sūta uvāca
snātvā devaṃ namaskṛtya devadevamumāpatim  /
divyena cakṣuṣārudrāṃ nīlalohitamīśvaram  // 2,28.1 //
dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭāva varadaṃ rudrādhyāyena śaṅkaram  /
devo 'pi tuṣṭyā nirvāṇaṃ rājyānte karmaṇaiva tu  // 2,28.2 //
tavā stīti sakṛccoktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata  /
svāyaṃbhuvo manurdevaṃ namaskṛtya vṛṣadhvajam  // 2,28.3 //
āruroha mahāmeruṃ mahāvṛṣamiveśvaraḥ  /
tatra devaṃ hiramyābhaṃ yogaiśvaryasamanvitam  // 2,28.4 //
sanatkumāraṃ varadamapaśyadbrahmaṇaḥ sutam  /
namaścakāra varadaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ brahmarūpiṇam  // 2,28.5 //
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tuṣṭāva ca mahādyutiḥ  /
so 'pi dṛṣṭvā manuṃ devo hṛṣṭaromābhavanmuniḥ  // 2,28.6 //
sanatkumāraḥ prāhedaṃ ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇānidhe  /
sanatkumāra uvāca
dṛṣṭvā sarveśvarācchāntācchaṅkarānnīlalohitāt  // 2,28.7 //
labdhvābhiṣekaṃ saṃprāpto vivakṣurvada yadyapi  /
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ  // 2,28.8 //
vijñāpayāmāsa kathaṃ karmaṇā nirvṛtirvibho  /
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ karmaṇā kevalena ca  // 2,28.9 //
jñānena nirvṛtiḥ siddhā vibho miśreṇa vā kkacit  /
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā śrutisāravidāṃ nidhiḥ  // 2,28.10 //
sanatkumāro bhagavānkarmaṇā nirvṛtiṅkramāt  /
miśreṇa ca kramādeva kṣaṇājjñānena vai mune  // 2,28.11 //
purāmānena coṣṭratvamagamaṃ nandinaḥ prabhoḥ  /
śāpātpunaḥ prasādāddhi śivamabhyarcya śaṅkaram  // 2,28.12 //
prasādānnandinastasya karmaṇaiva sutohyaham  /
śrutvottamāṃ gatiṃ divyāmavasthāṃ prāptavānaham  // 2,28.13 //
śivārcanaprakāreṇa śivadharmeṇa nānyathā  /
rājñāṃ ṣoḍaśadānāni nandinā kathitāni ca  // 2,28.14 //
dharmakāmārthamuktyarthaṃ karmaṇaiva mahātmanā  /
tulādirohaṇādyāni śṛṇu tāni yatātatham  // 2,28.15 //
grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu śubhadeśeṣu śobhanam  /
viṃśaddhastapramāṇena maṇḍapaṃ kūṭameva ca  // 2,28.16 //
yathāṣṭādaśahastena kalāhastena vā punaḥ  /
kṛtvā vediṃ tathā madhye navahastapramāṇataḥ  // 2,28.17 //
aṣṭahastena vā kāryā saptahastena vā punaḥ  /
dvihastā sārdhahastā vā vedikā cātiśobhanā  // 2,28.18 //
dvādaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktā sādhuramyā bhramantikā  /
parito nava kuṇḍāni caturasrāṇi kārayet  // 2,28.19 //
endrikeśānayormadhye pradhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutā  /
athavā caturasraṃ ca yonyākāramataḥ param  // 2,28.20 //
strīṇāṃ kuṇḍāni viprendrā yonyākārāṇi kārayet  /
ardhacandraṃ trikoṇaṃ ca vartulaṃ kuṇḍameva ca  // 2,28.21 //
ṣaḍasraṃ sarvato vāpi trikoṇaṃ padmasannibham  /
aṣṭāsraṃ sarvamāne tu sthaṇḍilaṃ kevalaṃ tu vā  // 2,28.22 //
caturdvārasamopetaṃ catustoraṇabhūṣitam  /
diggajāṣṭakasaṃyuktaṃ darbhamālāsamāvṛtam  // 2,28.23 //
aṣṭamaṅgalasaṃyuktaṃ vitānopariśobhitam  /
tulāstaṃbhadrumāścātra bilvādīni viśeṣataḥ  // 2,28.24 //
bilvāśvatthapalāśādyāḥ kevalaṃ khādiraṃ tu vā  /
yena staṃbhaḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ tena sarvaṃ tu kārayet  // 2,28.25 //
athavā miśramārgeṇa veṇunā vā prakalpayet  /
aṣṭahastapramāṇaṃ tu hastadvayasamāyutam  // 2,28.26 //
tulāstaṃbhasya viṣkaṃbho 'nāhatastriguṇomataḥ  /
dvyaṅgulena vihīnaṃ tu suvṛttaṃ nirvraṇaṃ tathā  // 2,28.27 //
ubhayorantaraṃ caiva ṣaḍḍhastaṃ nṛpate smṛtam  /
dvoyaścaturhastakṛtamantaraṃ staṃbhayorapi  // 2,28.28 //
ṣaḍastamantaraṃ jñeyaṃ staṃbhayorupari sthitam  /
vitāstimātraṃ vistāro viṣkaṃbhastāvaduttaram  // 2,28.29 //
staṃbhayostu pramāṇena uttaradvārasammitam  /
ṣaṭtriṃśanmātrasaṃyuktaṃ vyāyāmaṃ tu tulātmakam  // 2,28.30 //
viṣkaṃbhamaṣṭamātraṃ tu yavapaṇṭakasaṃyutam  /
ṣaṭtriṃśanmātranābhaṃ syānnirmāṇādvartulaṃ śubham  // 2,28.31 //
agre mūle ca madhye ca hemapaṭṭena bandayet  /
paṭṭamadhye prakartavyamavalaṃbanakatrayam  // 2,28.32 //
tāmreṇa ca prakartavyamavalaṃbanakatrayam  /
āreṇa vā prakartavyamāyasaṃ naiva kārayet  // 2,28.33 //
madhye cordhvamukhaṃ kāryamavalaṃbaḥ suśobhanaḥ  /
raśmibhistoraṇāgre vā bandhayecca vidhānataḥ  // 2,28.34 //
jihvāmekāṃ tulāmadhye tāreṇaṃ tu vidhīyate  /
uttarasya ca madhye ca śaṅkuṃ dṛḍhamanuttamam  // 2,28.35 //
vitānenopari cchādya dṛḍhaṃ samyakprayojayet  /
saṃkoḥ suṣirasaṃpannaṃ valayaṃ kārayenmune  // 2,28.36 //
tulāmadhye vitānena tulayālaṃbake tathā  /
valayena prayoktavyaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ vāvalaṃbanam  // 2,28.37 //
sudṛḍhaṃ ca tulāmadhye navamāṅgulamānataḥ  /
paṭṭasyaiva tu vistāraṃ pañcamātrapramāṇataḥ  // 2,28.38 //
aparau sudṛḍhau piṇḍau śubhadravyeṇa kārayet  /
śikyādhastātprakartavyau pañcaprādeśa vistarau  /
sahasreṇa tu kartavyau palānāṃ dhārakāvubhau  // 2,28.39 //
śataṣṭakena vā kuryātpalaiḥ ṣaṭśatameva vā  /
catustālaṃ ca kartavyo vistāromadyamastathā  // 2,28.40 //
sārdhatritālavistāraḥ kalaśasya vidhiyate  /
badhnīyātpañcapātraṃ tu trimātraṃ ṣaṭkamucyate  // 2,28.41 //
caturdvārasamopetaṃ dvāramaṅgulamātrakam  /
kuṇḍalaiśca samopetaiḥ śuklaśuddhasamanvitaiḥ  // 2,28.42 //
kuṇḍalekuṇḍale kāryaṃ śṛṅkhalāparimaṇḍalam  /
śṛṅkhalādhāravalayamavalaṃ bena yojayet  // 2,28.43 //
prādeśaṃ vā caturmātraṃ bhūmestyaktvāvalaṃbayet  /
ghaṭau puruṣamātrau tu kartavyau śobhanāvubhau  // 2,28.44 //
tau vālukābhiḥ saṃpūrya śivaṃ tatra viniḥkṣipet  /
dvihastamātramavaṭe sthāpanīyau prayatnataḥ  // 2,28.45 //
niḥśeṣaṃ pūrayodvidvānvālukābhiḥ samantataḥ  /
yena niścalatāṃ gacchettena mārgeṇa kārayet  // 2,28.46 //
śrūyatāṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ vedikoparimaṇḍalam  /
aṣṭamāṅgulasaṃyuktaṃ maṅgalākuraśobhitam  // 2,28.47 //
phalapuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ dhūpadīpasamanvitam  /
vedimadhye prakartavyaṃ darpaṇodarasannibham  // 2,28.48 //
ālikhenmaṇḍalaṃ pūrvaṃ caturdvārasamanvitam  /
śobhopaśobhāsaṃpannaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam  // 2,28.49 //
varṇajātisamopetaṃ pañcavarṇaṃ tu kārayet  /
vajraṃ prāgantare bhāge āgneyyāṃ śaktimujjvalām  // 2,28.50 //
ālikheddakṣiṇe daṇḍaṃ nairṛtyāṃ khaṅgamālikhet  /
pāśaśca vāruṇe lekhyo dhvajaṃ vai vāyugocare  // 2,28.51 //
kauberyāṃ tu gadā lekhyā aiśānyāṃ śūlamālikhet  /
śūlasya vāmadeśena cakraṃ padmaṃ tu dakṣiṇe  // 2,28.52 //
evaṃ likhitvā paścācca homakarmasamācaret  /
pradhānahomaṃ gāyatryā svāhā śakraāya vahneye  // 2,28.53 //
yamāya rākṣaseśāya varuṇāya ca vāyave  /
kuberāyeśvarāyātha viṣṇave brahmaṇe punaḥ  // 2,28.54 //
svāhāntaṃ praṇavenaiva hotavyaṃ vidhipūrvakam  /
svaśākhāgnimukhenaiva jayādipratisaṃyutam  // 2,28.55 //
sviṣṭāntaṃ sarvakāryāṇi kārayedvidhivattadā  /
sarvahomāgrahome ca samitpālāśamucyate  /
ekaviṃśatisaṃkhyātaṃ mantreṇānena homayet  // 2,28.56 //
ayantaidhmaātmājātavedastene dhyasvavardhasvaceddhavardhayacāsmānprajayāpaśubhirbrahmavarcasenānnādyenasamedhayasvāhā bhūḥ svāhā bhuvaḥsvāhā svaḥ svāhā bhūrbhuvaḥ svastathaiva ca  /
samiddhomaśca caruṇā ghṛtasya ca yathākramam  /
śuklānnapāyasaṃ caiva mudgānnaṃ caravaḥ smṛtāḥ  // 2,28.57 //
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā  // 2,28.58 //
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa āsuvorjamiṣaṃ ca naḥ  /
arobādhasvaducchanām  /
agnirṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pāñcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ  /
tamīmahe mahāgayam  /
agne pavasva svapā asme varcaḥ suvīryam  /
dadhadrayiṃ mayi poṣam  /
prajāpate na tvadetānyanyo viśvājātāni paritā babhūva  /
yatkāmāste juhumastanno astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām  /
gāyatryā ca pradhānasya samiddhomastathaiva va  /
caruṇā ca tathājyasya śakradīnāṃ ca homayet  // 2,28.59 //
vajrādīnāṃ ca hotavyaṃ sahasrārdhaṃ tataḥ kramāt  /
brahma jajñeti mantreṇa brahmaṇe viṣṇave punaḥ  // 2,28.60 //
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsu devāya dhīmahi  /
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt  /
ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathito homamārgaḥ suśobhanaḥ  /
dūrvayā kṣīrayuktena pañcaviṃśatpṛthakpṛthak  // 2,28.61 //
tryaṃbakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam  /
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyormukṣayi māmṛtāt  // 2,28.62 //
dūrvāhomaḥ praśasto 'yaṃ vāsuhomaśca sarvathā  /
prāyaścittamaghoreṇa sarpiṣā ca śataṃśatam  // 2,28.63 //
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe vāme viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ śivam  /
madhye devyā samaṃ jñeyamindrādigaṇasaṃvṛtam  // 2,28.64 //
ādityaṃ bhāskaraṃ bhānuṃ raviṃ devaṃ divākaram  /
uṣāṃ prabhāṃ tathā prajñāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sāvitrimeva ca  // 2,28.65 //
pañcaprakāravidhinā khakholkāya mahātmane  /
viṣṭarāṃ subhagāṃ caiva vardhanīṃ ca pradakṣiṇām  // 2,28.66 //
āpyāyanīṃ ca saṃpūjya devī padmāsane ravim  /
prabhūtaṃ vātha kartavyaṃ vimalaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā  // 2,28.67 //
sāraṃ paścimabhāge ca ārādhyaṃ cottare yajet  /
madhye sukhaṃ vijānīyātkesareṣu yathākramam  // 2,28.68 //
dīptāṃ sūkṣmāṃ jayāṃ bhadrāṃ vibhūtiṃ vimalāṃ kramāt  /
amoghāṃ vidyutāṃ caiva madhyataḥ sarvatomukhīm  // 2,28.69 //
somamaṅgārakaṃ caiva budhaṃ gurumanukramāt  /
bhārgavaṃ ca tathā mandaṃ rāhuṃ ketuṃ tathaiva ca  // 2,28.70 //
pūjayeddhomayedevaṃ dāpayecca viśeṣataḥ  /
yogino bhojayettatra śivatattvaikapāragān  // 2,28.71 //
divyādhyayanasaṃpannānkṛtvaivaṃ vidhivistaram  /
home pravartamāne ca pūrvādiksthānamadhyame  // 2,28.72 //
ārohayedvidhānena rudrādhyāyena vai nṛpam  /
dārayettatra bhūpālaṃ ghaṭikaikāṃ vidānataḥ  // 2,28.73 //
yajamāno japenmantraṃ rudragāyatrisaṃjñakam  /
ghaṭikārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tatraivāsanāmārabhet  // 2,28.74 //
ālokya vāruṇaṃ dhīmānkūrcahastaḥ samāhitaḥ  /
nṛpaśca bhūṣaṇairyuktaḥ khaḍgakheṭakadhārakaḥ  // 2,28.75 //
svastirityādibhiścādāvante caiva viśeṣataḥ  /
puṇyāhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ  // 2,28.76 //
jayamaṅgalaśabdādibrahmaghoṣaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ  /
nṛtyavādyādibhirgītaiḥ sarvaśobhāsamanvitaiḥ  // 2,28.77 //
svamevaṃ candradigbhāge suvarṇaṃ tatra vikṣipet  /
tulādhārau samau vṛttau tulābhāraḥ sadā bhavet  // 2,28.78 //
śataniṣkādhikaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tadardhaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam  /
tasyārdhaṃ ca kaniṣṭhaṃ syāttrividhaṃ tatra kalpitam  // 2,28.79 //
vastrayugmamathoṣṇīṣaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ kaṇṭhaśobhanam  /
aṅgulībhīṣaṇaṃ caiva maṇibandhasya bhūṣaṇam  // 2,28.80 //
etāni caiva sarvāṇi prāraṃbhe dharmakarmaṇi  /
pāśupatavratāyātha bhasmāṅgāya pradāpayet  // 2,28.81 //
pūrvoktabhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ soṣṇīṣaṃ vastrasaṃyutam  /
dadyādetatprayoktubhya ācchādanapaṭaṃ budhaḥ  // 2,28.82 //
dakṣiṇāṃ ca śataṃ sārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā pradāpayet  /
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet  // 2,28.83 //
yāgopakaraṇaṃ divyamācāryāya pradāpayet  /
itareṣāṃ yatīnāṃ tu pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet  // 2,28.84 //
tulāroha suvarṇaṃ ca śivāya vinivedayet  /
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ caiva prākāraṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā  // 2,28.85 //
suvarṇapuṣpaṃ paṭahaṃ khaḍgaṃ vai kośameva ca  /
kṛtvā dattvā śivāyātha kiñciccheṣaṃ ca buddhimān  // 2,28.86 //
ācāryebhyaḥ pradātavyaṃ bhasmāṅgebhyo viśeṣataḥ  /
payasā vātha dadhnā vā sarvadravyairathāpi vā  /
brahmakūrcena vā devaṃ pañcagavyena cavā punaḥ  // 2,28.87 //
sahasrakalaśaistatra secayetparameśvaram  /
ghṛtena kevalenāpi devadevamumāpatim  // 2,28.88 //
payasā vātha dadhnā vā sarvadravyairathāpi vā  /
brahmakūrcena vā devaṃ pañcagavyena vā punaḥ  // 2,28.89 //
gāyatryā caiva gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ praṇavena vā  /
āpyāyasveti vai kṣīraṃ dadhikraāvṇoti vai dadhi  // 2,28.90 //
tejosītyājyamīśānamantreṇaivābhiṣecayet  /
devasyatvoti deveśaṃ kuśāṃbukalaśena vai  // 2,28.91 //
rudrādhyāyena vā sarvaṃ snāpayetparameśvaram  /
sahasrakalaśaṃ śaṃbhornāmnāṃ caiva sahasrakaiḥ  // 2,28.92 //
viṣṇunā kathitairvāpi taṇḍinā kathitaistu vā  /
dakṣeṇa munimukhyena kīrtitairathavā punaḥ  // 2,28.93 //
mahāpūjā prakartavyā mahādevasya bhaktitaḥ  /
śivārcakāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā svaguroḥ sadā  // 2,28.94 //
dehārṇavaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ dakṣiṇā ca yatākramam  /
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāṃ ca bālavṛddhakṛsāturān  // 2,28.95 //
bhojayecca vidhānena dakṣiṇāmapi dāpayet  // 2,28.96 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tulāpuruṣadānavidhāvaṣṭāviṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
tulā te kathitā hyeṣā ādyā sāmānyarūpiṇī  /
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ vakṣyāmi dvitīyaṃ sarvasiddhidam  // 2,29.1 //
adhaḥ pātraṃ sahasreṇa hiraṇyena vidhīyate  /
ūrdhvapātraṃ tadardhena mukhaṃ saṃveśamātrakam  // 2,29.2 //
haimamevaṃ śubhaṃ kuryāt sarvālaṃkārasaṃyutam  /
adhaḥ pātre smareddevīṃ guṇatrayasamanvitām  // 2,29.3 //
caturviśatikāṃ devīṃ brahmaviṣṇvagnirūpiṇīm  /
ūrdhvapātre guṇātītaṃ ṣaḍviśakamumāpatim  // 2,29.4 //
ātmānaṃ puruṣaṃ dhyāyetpañcaviśakamagrajam  /
pūrvoktasthānamadhye 'tha vedikopari maṇḍale  // 2,29.5 //
śālīmadhye kṣipennītvā navavastraiśca veṣṭayet  /
māṣakalkena cāliṣya pañcadravyeṇa pūjayet  // 2,29.6 //
īśānādyairyathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ paripūjayet  /
pūrvavacchivapūjā ca homaścaiva yathakramam  // 2,29.7 //
devīṃ gāyatrikāṃ japtvā praviśetprāṅmukhaḥ svayam  /
vidhinaiva tu saṃpādya garbhādhānādikāṃ kriyām  // 2,29.8 //
kṛtvā ṣoḍaśamārgeṇa vidhinā brāhmaṇottamaḥ  /
dūrvākuraistu kartavyā secanā dakṣiṇe puṭe  // 2,29.9 //
auduṃbaraphalaiḥ sārdham ekaviṃśatkuśodakam  /
īśānyāṃ tāvadevātra kuryātsīmantakarmaṇi  // 2,29.10 //
udvahetkanyakāṃ kṛtvā triṃśanniṣkeṇa śobhanām  /
alaṅkṛtya tathā hutvā śivāya vinivedayet  // 2,29.11 //
annaprāśanake vidvān bhojayetpāyasādibhiḥ  /
evaṃ viśvajitāntā vai garbhādhānādikāḥ kriyāḥ  // 2,29.12 //
śaktibījena kartavyā brāhmaṇairvedapāragaiḥ  /
śeṣaṃ sarvaṃ ca vidhivattulāhemavadācaret  // 2,29.13 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi tilaparvatamuttamam  /
pūrvoktasthānakāle tu kṛtvā saṃpūjya yatnataḥ  // 2,30.1 //
susame bhūtale ramye vedinā ca vivarjite  /
daśatālapramāṇaena daṇḍaṃ saṃsthāpya vai mune  // 2,30.2 //
adbhiḥ saṃprokṣya paścāddhi tilāṃstvasminvinikṣipet  /
pañcagavyena taṃ deśaṃ prokṣayedbrāhmaṇottamaḥ  // 2,30.3 //
maṇḍalaṃ kalpayedvidvānpūrvavatsusamantataḥ  /
navavastraiśca saṃsthāpya ramyapuṣpairvikīrya ca  // 2,30.4 //
tasminsaṃcayanaṃ kāryaṃ tilabhārairviśeṣataḥ  /
daṇḍaprādeśamutsedhamuttamaṃ parikīrtitam  // 2,30.5 //
caturaṅgulahīnaṃ tu madhyamaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ  /
daṇḍatulyaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ syāddaṇḍahīnaṃ na kārayet  // 2,30.6 //
veṣṭayitvā navairvastraiḥ paritaḥ pūjayetkramāt  /
sadyādīni pravinyasya pūjayedvidhipūrvakam  // 2,30.7 //
aṣṭadikṣu ca kartavyāḥ pūrvoktā mūrtayaḥ kramāt  /
triniṣkena suvarṇena pratyekaṃ kārayetkramāt  // 2,30.8 //
dakṣiṇā vidhinā kāryā tulābhāravadeva tu  /
homaścapūrvavatprokto yathāvanmunisattamāḥ  // 2,30.9 //
arcayeddevadeveśaṃ lokapālasamāvṛtam  /
tilaparvatamadhyasthaṃ tilaparvatarūpiṇam  // 2,30.10 //
śivārcanā ca kartavyā sahasrakalaśādibhiḥ  /
darśayettilamadhyasthaṃ devadevamumāpatim  // 2,30.11 //
pūjayitvā vidhānena krameṇa ca visarjayet  /
śrotriyāya daridrāya dāpayettilaparvatam  // 2,30.12 //
evaṃ tilanagaḥ proktaḥ sarvasmādadhikaḥ paraḥ  // 2,30.13 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tilaparvatadānaṃ nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyaṃ parvataṃ sūkṣmamalpadravyaṃ mahāphalam  /
dravyamātropasaṃyukte kāle madhyaṃ vidhīyate  // 2,31.1 //
gomayāliptabhūmau tu hyaṃbarāṇi prakīrya ca  /
tanmadhye nikṣipeddhīmāṃstilabhāratrayaṃ śubham  // 2,31.2 //
padmamaṣṭadalaṃ kuryātkarṇikākesarānvitam  /
daśaniṣkeṇa tatkāryaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ  // 2,31.3 //
tilamadhye nyasetpadmaṃ padmamadhye maheśvaram  /
ārādhya vidhivaddevaṃ vāmādīni prapūjayet  // 2,31.4 //
śaktirūpaṃ suvarṇena triniṣkeṇa tu kārayet  /
nyāsaṃ tu paritaḥ kuryādvighneśānparibhāgataḥ  // 2,31.5 //
pūrvokta hemamānena vighneśānapi kārayet  /
tān abhyarcya vidhānena gandhapūṣpādibhiḥ kramāt  // 2,31.6 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
japahomārcanādānābhiṣekādyaṃ ca pūrvavat  /
muvarṇamedinīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ  // 2,32.1 //
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu kārayenmunibhiḥ saha  /
lakṣaṇena yathāpūrvaṃ kuṇḍe vā maṇḍale 'tha vā  // 2,32.2 //
medinīṃ kārayeddivyāṃ sahasreṇāpi vā punaḥ  /
ekahastā prakartavyā caturasrā suśobhanā  // 2,32.3 //
saptadvīpasamudrādyaiḥ parvatairabhisaṃvṛtā  /
sarvatīrthasamopetā madhye merusamanvitā  // 2,32.4 //
athavā madhyato dvīpaṃ navakhaṇḍaṃ prakalpayet  /
pūrvavannikilaṃ kṛtvā maṇḍale vedimadhyataḥ  // 2,32.5 //
saptabhāgaikabhāgena sahasrādvidhipūrvakam  /
śivabhakte pradātavyā dakṣiṇā pūrvacoditā  // 2,32.6 //
sahasrakalaśādyaiśca śaṅkaraṃ pūjayecchivam  /
suvarṇamedinīproktaṃ liṅgasmindānamuttamam  // 2,32.7 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇamedinīnīdānaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________



sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyatsaṃpravakṣyāmi kalpapādapamuttamam  /
śatāniṣkeṇa kṛtvaivaṃ sarvaśākhāsamanvitam  // 2,33.1 //
śākhānāṃ vividhaṃ kṛtvā muktā dāmādyalaṃbanam  /
divyairmārakataiścaiva cāṅkurāgraṃ pravinyaset  // 2,33.2 //
pravālaṃ kārayedvidvānpravālena drumasya tu  /
phalāni padmarāgaiśca parito 'sya suśobhayet  // 2,33.3 //
mūlaṃ ca nīlaratnena vajreṇa skandhamuttamam  /
vaiḍūryeṇa drumāgraṃ ca puṣparāgeṇa mastakam  // 2,33.4 //
gomedakena vai kandaṃ sūryakāntena suvrata  /
candrakāntena vā vedīṃ drumasya sphaṭikena vā  // 2,33.5 //
vitastimātramāyāmaṃ vṛkṣasya parikīrtitam  /
śākhāṣṭakasya mānaṃ ca vistāraṃ cordhvatastathā  // 2,33.6 //
tanmūle stāpayelliṅgaṃ lokapālaiḥ samāvṛtam  /
pūrvoktavedimadhye tu maṇḍale sthāpya pādapam  // 2,33.7 //
pūjaye ddevamīśānaṃ lokapālāṃśca yatnataḥ  /
pūrvavajjapahomādyaṃ tulābhāravadācaret  // 2,33.8 //
nivedayeddrumaṃ śaṃbhoryogināṃ vātha vā nṛpa  /
bhasmāṅgibhyo 'thavā rājā sārvabhaumo bhaviṣyati  // 2,33.9 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kalpapādapadānavidirnāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
gaṇeśeśaṃ pravakṣyāmi dānaṃ pūrvoktamaṇḍape  /
saṃpūjya devadevesaṃ lokapālasamāvṛtam  // 2,34.1 //
viśveśvarānyathāśāstraṃ sarvābharaṇasaṃyutān  /
daśaniṣkeṇa vai kṛtvā saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ  // 2,34.2 //
aṣṭadakṣvaṣṭakuṇḍeṣu pūrvavaddhomamācaret  /
pañcāvaraṇamārgeṇa pāraṃparyakrameṇa ca  // 2,34.3 //
saptaviprānsamabhyarcya kanyāmekāṃ tathottare  /
dāpayetsarvamantrāṇi svaiḥsvairmantrairanukramāt  // 2,34.4 //
dattvaivaṃ sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  // 2,34.5 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gaṇeśeśadānavidinirūpaṇaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
atha te saṃpravakṣyāmi hemadhenuvidhikramam  /
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ grahadurbhikṣanāśanam  // 2,35.1 //
upasargapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhi nivāraṇam  /
niṣkāṇāṃ ca sahasreṇa suvarṇena tu kārayet  // 2,35.2 //
tadardhenāpi vā samyak tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ  /
śatena vā prakartavyā sarvarūpaguṇānvitā  // 2,35.3 //
gorūpaṃ sukhuraṃ divyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam  /
khurāgre vinyasedvajraṃ śṛṅge vai padmarāgakam  // 2,35.4 //
bhruvormadhye nyaseddivyaṃ mauktikaṃ munisattamāḥ  /
vauḍūryeṇa stanāḥ kāryā lāṅgūlaṃ nīlataḥ subham  // 2,35.5 //
dantasthāne prakartavyaḥ puṣparāgaḥ suśobhanaḥ  /
paśuvatkārayitvā tu vatsaṃ kuryātsuśobhanam  // 2,35.6 //
suvarṇadaśaniṣkeṇa sarvaratnasuśobhitam  /
pūrvoktavedikāmadhye maṇḍalaṃ parikalpya tu  // 2,35.7 //
tanmadhye surabhiṃ sthāpya savatsāṃ sarvatattvavit  /
savatsāṃ surabhiṃ tatra vastrayugmena veṣṭayet  // 2,35.8 //
saṃpūjayedgāṃ gāyatryā savatsāṃ surabhiṃ punaḥ  /
athaikāgnividhānena homaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi  // 2,35.9 //
samidājyavidhānena pūrvavaccheṣamācaret  /
śivapūjā prakartavyā liṅgaṃ snāpya ghṛtādibhiḥ  // 2,35.10 //
gāmālabhya ca gāyatryā śivāyādāpayecchubhām  /
dakṣiṇā ca prakartavyā triṃśanniṣkā mahāmate  // 2,35.11 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hemadhenudānavidhinīrūpaṇaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
lakṣmīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi mahadaiśvaryavardhanam  /
pūrvoktamaṇḍapekāryaṃ vedikoparimaṇḍale  // 2,36.1 //
śrīdevīmatulāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi  /
sahasreṇa tadardhena tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ  // 2,36.2 //
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām  /
maṇḍale vinyasellakṣmīṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutām  // 2,36.3 //
tasyāstu dakṣiṇe bhāge sthaṇḍile viṣṇumarcayet  /
arcayitvā vidhānena śrīsuktena sureśvarīm  // 2,36.4 //
arcayedviṣṇugāyatryā viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ harim  /
ārādhya vidhinā devīṃ pūrvavaddhoma mācaret  // 2,36.5 //
samiddhrutvā vidhānena ājyāhutimathācaret  /
pṛthagaṣṭotaraśataṃ homayed brāhmaṇottamaiḥ  // 2,36.6 //
āhūya yajamānaṃ tu tasyāḥ pūrvadiśi sthale  /
tasmai tāṃ darśayeddevīṃ daṇḍavatpraṇamotkṣitau  // 2,36.7 //
praṇamya viṣṇuṃ tatrasthaṃ śivaṃ pūrvavadarcayet  /
tasyā viṃśatibhāgaṃ tu dakṣiṇā parikīrtitā  // 2,36.8 //
tadardhāṃśaṃ tu dātavyamitareṣāṃ yathārhataḥ  /
tatastu homayecchaṃbhuṃ bhakto yogī viśeṣataḥ  // 2,36.9 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge lakṣmīdānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumārā uvāca
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tiladhenuvidhikramam  /
pūrvoktamaṇḍape kuryācchivapūjāṃ tu paścime  // 2,37.1 //
tasyāgre madhyato bhūmau padmamālikhya śobhanam  /
vastrairācchāditaṃ padmaṃ tanmadhye vinyasecchubham  // 2,37.2 //
tilapuṣpaṃ tu kṛtvātha hemapadmaṃ vinikṣipet  /
triṃśanniṣkema kartavyaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ  // 2,37.3 //
pañcaniṣkeṇa kartavyaṃ tadardhārhdena vā punaḥ  /
tamārādhya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt  // 2,37.4 //
padmasyottaradigbhāge viprānekādaśanyaset  /
tānabhyarcya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt  // 2,37.5 //
ācchādanottarāsaṃgaṃ viprebhyo dāpayetkramāt  /
uṣṇīṣaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ kuṇḍaleca vibhūṣite  // 2,37.6 //
hemāṅgulīyakaṃ dattvā brāhmaṇebhyo vidhānataḥ  /
ekaṃ daśa ca vastrāṇiṃ teṣāmagre prakīrya ca  // 2,37.7 //
teṣu vastreṣu niḥkṣipyatilādyāni pṛthakpṛthak  /
kāṃsyapātraṃ śatapalaṃ vibhidyaikādaśāṃśakam  // 2,37.8 //
ikṣudaṇḍaṃ ca dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ  /
gośṛge tu hiraṇyena dvinīṣkeṇa tu kārayet  // 2,37.9 //
rajatena tu kartavyāḥ khurā niṣkadvayena tu  /
evaṃ pṛthakpṛthag dattvā tattileṣu vinikṣipet  // 2,37.10 //
rudraikādaśamantraistu rudrebhyo dāpayettadā  /
padmasya pūrvadigbhāge viprāndvādaśa pūjitān  // 2,37.11 //
etenaiva tu mārgeṇa teṣu śraddhāsamanvitaḥ  /
dvādaśādhityamantraiśca dāpayedevameva ca  // 2,37.12 //
pūrvavaddakṣiṇe bhāge viprānṣoḍaśa saṃsthitān  /
mūrti vighneśamantraiśca dāpayetpūrvavatpunaḥ  // 2,37.13 //
yajamānena kartavyaṃ sarvametadyathākramam  /
kevalaṃ rudradānaṃ vā adityebhyo 'tha vā punaḥ  // 2,37.14 //
mūrtyādīnāṃ ca vā deyaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram  /
padmaṃ vinyasya rājāsau śeṣaṃ vā kārayennṛpaḥ  // 2,37.15 //
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā pañcaniṣkeṇa bhūṣaṇam  // 2,37.16 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tiladhenudānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
gosahasrapradānaṃ ca vadāmi śṛṇu suvrata  /
gavāṃ sahasramādāya savatsaṃ saguṇaṃ śubham  // 2,38.1 //
tās tv abhyarcya yathāśāstram aṣṭau samyakprayatnataḥ  /
tāsāṃ śṛṅgāṇi hemnātha pratiniṣkeṇa bandhayet  // 2,38.2 //
khurāṃśca rajatenaiva bandayetkaṇṭhadesataḥ  /
pratiniṣkeṇa kartavyaṃ karṇe vajraṃ ca śobhanam  // 2,38.3 //
śivāya dadyādviprebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak  /
daśaniṣkaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tasyārdhārdhamathāpi vā  // 2,38.4 //
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ niṣkamātramathāpi vā  /
vastrayugmaṃ ca dātavyaṃ pṛthagvipreṣu śobhanam  // 2,38.5 //
gāvaścārādhya yatnena dātavyāḥ sumanoramāḥ  /
evaṃ dattvā vidhānena śivamabhyarcya saṃkaram  // 2,38.6 //
japedagre yathānyāyaṃ gavāṃ stavamanuttamam  /
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvo naḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā  // 2,38.7 //
hṛdaye me sadā gāvo gāvaṃ madhye vasāmy aham  /
iti kṛtvā dvijāgryebhyodattvā gatvā pradakṣiṇam  // 2,38.8 //
tadromavarṣasaṃkhyāni svargaloke mahīyate  // 2,38.9 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gosahasrapradānaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
hiraṇyāśvapradānaṃ ca vadāmī vijayāvaham  /
aśvamedhātpunaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ vadāmī śṛṇu suvrata  // 2,39.1 //
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa aṣṭottaraśatena vā  /
kṛtvāśvaṃ lakṣaṇairyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam  // 2,39.2 //
pañcakalyāṇasaṃpannaṃ divyākāraṃ tu kārayet  /
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvāṅgaiśca samanvitam  // 2,39.3 //
sarvāyudhasamopetamindravāhanamuttamam  /
tanmadhyadeśe saṃsthāpya turaṅgaṃ svaguṇānvitam  // 2,39.4 //
uccaiḥ śravasakaṃ matvā bhaktyā caiva samarcayet  /
tasya pūrvādiśābhāge brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam  // 2,39.5 //
suredrabuddhyā saṃpūjya pañcaniṣkaṃ pradāpayet  /
sa cāśvaḥ śivabhaktāya dātavyo vidhinaiva tu  // 2,39.6 //
suvarṇāśvaṃ pradattvā tu ācāryamapi pūjayet  /
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ pañcaniṣkamathāpivā  // 2,39.7 //
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāthabālavṛddhakṛśāturān  /
toṣayedannadānena brāhmaṇāṃśca viśeṣataḥ  // 2,39.8 //
etadyaḥ kurute bhaktyā dānamaśvasya mānavaḥ  /
eendrānbhogāṃściraṃ bhuktvā ruciraiśvaryavānbhavet  // 2,39.9 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hiraṇyāśvadānaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
kanyādānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvadānottamottamam  /
kanyāṃ lakṣaṇasaṃpannāṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitām  // 2,40.1 //
mātāpitrostu saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā dattvā dhanaṃ mahat  /
ātmīkṛtyātha saṃsnāpya vastraṃ dattvā śubhaṃ navam  // 2,40.2 //
bhūṣaṇairbhūṣayitvātha gandhamālyairathārcayet  /
nimittāni samīkṣyātha gotranakṣatrakādikān  // 2,40.3 //
ubhayościttamālokya ubhau saṃpūjya yatnataḥ  /
dātavyā śrotriyāyaiva brāhmaṇāya tapasvine  // 2,40.4 //
sākṣādadhītavedāya vidhinā brahmacāriṇe  /
dāsadāsīdhanāḍhyaṃ ca bhūṣaṇāniṃ viśeṣataḥ  // 2,40.5 //
kṣetrāṇi ca dhanaṃ dhānya vāsāṃsi ca pradāpayet  /
yāvanti dehe romāṇi kanyāyāḥ saṃtatau punaḥ  // 2,40.6 //
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate  // 2,40.7 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kanyādānavidhirnāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
hiraṇyavṛṣadānaṃ ca kathayāmi samāsataḥ  /
vṛṣarūpaṃ hiraṇyena sahasreṇātha kārayet  // 2,41.1 //
tadardhārdhena vā dhīmāṃstadardhārdhena vā punaḥ  /
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi vṛṣabhaṃ dharmarūpiṇam  // 2,41.2 //
lalāṭe kārayetpuṇḍramardhacandrakalākṛtim  /
sphaṭikena tu karttavyaṃ khuraṃ tu rajatena vai  // 2,41.3 //
grīvāṃ tu padmarāgeṇa kakudgomedakena ca  /
grīvāyāṃ ghāṇṭavalayaṃ ratnacitraṃ tu kārayet  // 2,41.4 //
vṛṣāṅkaṃ kārayettatra kiṅkiṇīvalayāvṛtam  /
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu vedikoparimaṇḍale  // 2,41.5 //
vṛṣendraṃ sthāpayettatra paścimāmukhamagrataḥ  /
īśvaraṃ pūjayedbhaktyā vṛṣārūḍhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam  // 2,41.6 //
vṛṣendraṃ pūjya gāyatryā namaskṛtya samāhitaḥ  /
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe dharmapādāya dhīmahi  /
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,41.7 //
mantreṇānena saṃpūjya vṛṣaṃ dharmavivṛddhaye  /
homayecca ghṛtānnādyairyathāvibhavavistaram  // 2,41.8 //
vṛṣabhaḥ pūjya dātavyo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śivāya vā  /
dakṣiṇā caiva dātavyā yathāvittānusārataḥ  // 2,41.9 //
etadyaḥ kurute bhaktyā vṛṣadānamanuttamam  /
śivasyānucaro bhūtvā tenaiva saha modate  // 2,41.10 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇavṛṣadānaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
gajadānaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  /
dvijāya vā śivāyātha dātavyaḥ pūjya pūrvavat  // 2,42.1 //
gajaṃ sulakṣaṇopetaṃ haimaṃ vā rājataṃ tu vā  /
sahasraniṣkamātreṇa tadardhenāpi kārayet  // 2,42.2 //
tadardhārdhena vā kuryātsarvalakṣaṇabhūṣitam  /
pūrvoktadeśakāle ca devāya vinivedayet  // 2,42.3 //
aṣṭamyāṃ vā pradātavyaṃ śivāya parameṣṭhine  /
brāhmaṇāya daridrāya śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye  // 2,42.4 //
śivamuddiśya dātavyaṃ śivaṃ saṃpūjya pūrvavat  /
etadyaḥ kurute dānaṃ śivabhaktisamāhitam  // 2,42.5 //
sthitvā svarge ciraṃ kālaṃ rājā gajapatirbhavet  // 2,42.6 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sanatkumāra uvāca
lokapālāṣṭakaṃ divyaṃ sākṣātparamadurlabham  /
sarvasaṃpatkaraṃ guhyaṃ paracakravināśanam  // 2,43.1 //
svadeśarakṣaṇaṃ divyaṃ gajavājivivardhanam  /
putra vṛddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ gobrāhmaṇahitāvaham  // 2,43.2 //
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu vedikoparimaṇḍale  /
madhye śivaṃ samabhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ yathākramam  // 2,43.3 //
digvidikṣu prakartavyaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vālukāmayam  /
aṣṭau viprānsamabhyarcya vedavedāṅgapāragān  // 2,43.4 //
jitendriyānkulodbhūtānsarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutān  /
śivābhimukhamāsīnānāhateṣvaṃbareṣu ca  // 2,43.5 //
vastrairābharaṇairdivyairlokapālakamantrakaiḥ  /
gandhapuṣpaiḥ sudhūpaiśca brāhmaṇānarcayetkramāt  // 2,43.6 //
pūrvato homayedagnau lokapālakamantrakaiḥ  /
samiddhṛtābhyāṃ hotavyamagnikāryaṃ krameṇa vā  // 2,43.7 //
evaṃ hutvā vidhānena ācāryaḥ śivavatsalaḥ  /
yajamānaṃ samāhūya sarvābharamabhūṣitān  // 2,43.8 //
tena tānpūjayitvātha dvijobhyo dāpayeddhanam  /
pṛthakpṛthaktanmantraiśca daśaniṣkaṃ ca bhūṣaṇam  // 2,43.9 //
daśanīṣkeṇa kartavyamāsanaṃ kevalaṃ pṛthak  /
snapanaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ śivasya vidhipūrvakam  // 2,43.10 //
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā yathāvibhavavistaram  /
evaṃ yaḥ kurute dānaṃ lokeśānāṃ tu bhaktitaḥ  /
lokeśānāṃ ciraṃ sthitvā sārvabhaumau bhavedbudhaḥ  // 2,43.11 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________

sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyatsaṃpravakṣyāmi sarvadānottamottamam  /
pūrvoktadeśakāle ca maṇḍape ca vidhānataḥ  // 2,44.1 //
praṇayātkuṇḍamadhye ca sthaṇḍile śivasannidhau  /
pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ samāsādya padmayonimataḥ param  // 2,44.2 //
mantrābhyāṃ vidhinoktābhyāṃ praṇavādisamantrakam  /
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi  /
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt  // 2,44.3 //
brahmabrāhmaṇavṛddhāya brahmaṇe viśvavedhase  /
śivāya haraye svāhā svadhā vauṣaṭvaṣaṭ tathā  // 2,44.4 //
pūjayitvā vidhānena paścāddhomaṃ samācaret  /
sarvadravyaṃ hi hotavyaṃ dvābhyāṃ kuṇḍavidhānataḥ  // 2,44.5 //
ṛtvijau dvau prakartavyau guruṇā vedapāragau  /
tānuddiśya yathānyāyaṃ viprebhyo dāpayeddhanam  // 2,44.6 //
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tebhyaḥ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamam  /
vastrābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam  // 2,44.7 //
gurureko hi vai śrīmān brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ  /
teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthagdeyaṃ bhojayedbrāhmaṇānapi  // 2,44.8 //
śivārcanā ca kartavyā snapanādi yathākramam  // 2,44.9 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ ṣoḍaśa dānāni kathitāni śubhāni ca  /
jīvacchrā ddhakramo 'smākaṃ vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam  // 2,45.1 //
sūta uvāca
jīvacchrāddhavidhiṃ vakṣye samāsātsarvasaṃmatam  /
manave devadevena kathitaṃ brahmaṇā purā  // 2,45.2 //
vasiṣṭhāsa ca śiṣṭāya bhṛgave bhārgavāya ca  /
śṛṇvantu sarvabhāvena sarvasiddhikaraṃ param  // 2,45.3 //
śrāddhamārgakramaṃ sākṣācchrāddhārhāṇāmapi kramam  /
viśeṣamapi vakṣyāmi jīvacchrāddhasya suvratāḥ  // 2,45.4 //
parvate vā nadītīre vane vāyatane 'pi vā  /
jīvacchrāddhaṃ prakartavyaṃ mṛtakāle prayatnataḥ  // 2,45.5 //
jīvacchrāddhe kṛte jīvo jīvanneva vimucyate  /
karma kurvannakurvanvā jñānī vājñānavānapi  // 2,45.6 //
śrotriyo 'śrotriyo vāpi brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo 'pi vā  /
vaiśyo vā nātra saṃdeho yogamārgagato yatā  // 2,45.7 //
parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ  /
śalyamuddhṛtya yatnena sthāṇḍilaṃ saikataṃ bhuvi  // 2,45.8 //
madhyato hastamātreṇa kuṇḍaṃ caivāyataṃ śubham  /
sthāṇḍilaṃ vā prakartavyamiṣumātraṃ punaḥ punaḥ  // 2,45.9 //
upalipya vidhānena cālipyāgniṃ vidhāya ca  /
anvādhāya yathāśāstraṃ parigṛhya ca sarvataḥ  // 2,45.10 //
paristīrya svaśākhoktaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam  /
samāpyāgnimukhaṃ sarvaṃ mantrairetairyathākramam  // 2,45.11 //
saṃpūjya sthaṇḍile vahnau homayetsamidādibhiḥ  /
ādau kṛtvā samiddhomaṃ caruṇā ca pṛthakpṛthak  // 2,45.12 //
ghṛtena ca pṛthakprātre śodhitena pṛthakpṛthak  /
juhuyādātmanoddhṛtya tattvabhūtāni sarvataḥ  // 2,45.13 //
oṃ bhūḥ brahmaṇe namaḥ  // 2,45.14 //
oṃ bhūḥ brahmaṇe svāhā  // 2,45.15 //
oṃ bhuvaḥ viṣṇave namaḥ  // 2,45.16 //
oṃ bhuvaḥ viṣṇave svāhā  // 2,45.17 //
oṃ svaḥ rudrāya namaḥ  // 2,45.18 //
oṃ svaḥ rudrāya svāhā  // 2,45.19 //
oṃ mahaḥ īśvarāya namaḥ  // 2,45.20 //
oṃ mahaḥ īśvarāya svāhā  // 2,45.21 //
oṃ janaḥ prakṛtaye namaḥ  // 2,45.22 //
oṃ janaḥ prakṛtaye svāhā  // 2,45.23 //
oṃ tapaḥ mudgalāya namaḥ  // 2,45.24 //
oṃ tapaḥ mudgalāya svāhā  // 2,45.25 //
oṃ ṛtaṃ puruṣāya namaḥ  // 2,45.26 //
oṃ ṛtaṃ paruṣāya svāhā  // 2,45.27 //
oṃ satyaṃ śivāya namaḥ  // 2,45.28 //
oṃ satyaṃ śivāya svāhā  // 2,45.29 //
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvāya devāya bhūrnamaḥ  // 2,45.30 //
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvāya bhūḥ svāhā  // 2,45.31 //
śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvasya devasya patnyai bhūrnamaḥ  // 2,45.32 //
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ sarvapatnyaibhūḥ svāhā  // 2,45.33 //
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyaṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvo namaḥ  // 2,45.34 //
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.35 //
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavasya devasya patnyai bhuvo namaḥ  // 2,45.36 //
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavasya patnyai bhuvaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.37 //
rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrāya devāya svarāeṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.38 //
rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrāya devāya svaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.39 //
rudrāgniṃ me gāpāya netre rūpaṃ rudrasya patnyai svarāeṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.40 //
rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrasya devasya patnyaisvaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.41 //
ugra vāyuṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśaṃ ugrāya devāya maharnamaḥ  // 2,45.42 //
ugra vāyūṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśamugrāya devāya mahaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.43 //
ugra vāyuṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśamugrasya devasya patnyai maharāeṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.44 //
oṃ ugra vāyuṃ mo gopāya tvaci sparśamugrasya devasya patnyai devāya janaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.45 //
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmāya devāya jano namaḥ  // 2,45.46 //
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmāya devāya janaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.47 //
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmasya patnyai jano namaḥ  // 2,45.48 //
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmasya devasya patnyai janaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.49 //
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇāmīśāya devāya tapo namaḥ  // 2,45.50 //
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇamīśāya devāya tapaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.51 //
rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇāmīśasya patnyai tapo namaḥ  // 2,45.52 //
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇamīśasya patnyai tapaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.53 //
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya ṛtaṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.54 //
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya ṛtaṃ svāhā  // 2,45.55 //
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya patnyai ṛtaṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.56 //
mahādeva satyaṃ ma gopāya śraddhāṃ mahādevasya patnyai ṛtaṃ svāhā  // 2,45.57 //
paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya bhoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupataye devāya satyaṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.58 //
paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya bhoktṛtvabhāgyaṃ paśupataye devasya satyaṃ svāhā  // 2,45.59 //
oṃ paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya yoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupater devasya patnyai satyaṃ namaḥ  // 2,45.60 //
oṃ paśupate pāśaṃ ma gopāya yoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupaterdevasya patnyai satyaṃ svāhā  // 2,45.61 //
oṃ śivāya namaḥ  // 2,45.62 //
oṃ śivāya satyaṃ svāhā  // 2,45.63 //
evaṃ śivāya hotavyaṃ viriñcyādyaṃ ca pūvavat  /
viriñcādyaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ sṛṣṭimārgeṣu suvratāḥ  // 2,45.64 //
punaḥ paśupateḥ patnīṃ tathā paśupatīṃ kramāt  /
saṃpūjya pūrvavanmantrairhetavyaṃ ca krameṇa vai  // 2,45.65 //
carvantamājyapūrvaṃ ca samidantaṃ samāhitaḥ  // 2,45.66 //
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me chindhi ghrāṇe gandhaṃ chindhi meghaṃ jahi bhūḥ svāhā  // 2,45.67 //
bhuvaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.68 //
svaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.69 //
bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.70 //
evaṃ pṛthakpṛthagghutvā kevalena ghṛtena vā  /
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā  // 2,45.71 //
virajā ca ghṛtenaiva śatamaṣṭottaraṃ pṛthak  /
prāṇādibhiśca juhuyāddhṛtenaiva tu kevalam  // 2,45.72 //
oṃ prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo ma viśāpradāhāya prāṇāya svāhā  // 2,45.73 //
prāṇādhipataye rudrāya vṛṣāntakāya svāhā  // 2,45.74 //
oṃ bhūḥ svāhā  // 2,45.75 //
oṃ bhuvaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.76 //
oṃ svaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.77 //
bhūrbhūvaḥ svaḥ svāhā  // 2,45.78 //
evaṃ krameṇa juhuyācchrāddhoktaṃ ca yatākramam  /
saptame 'hani yogīndrāñ chrāddhārhān api bhojayet  // 2,45.79 //
śarvādīnāṃ ca viprāṇāṃ vastrābharaṇakaṃbalān  /
vāhanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ kāṃsyatāmrādibhājanam  // 2,45.80 //
haimaṃ ca rājataṃ dhenuṃ tilān kṣetraṃ ca vaibhavam  /
dāsīdāsagaṇaścaiva dātavyo dakṣiṇāmapi  // 2,45.81 //
piṇḍaṃ ca pūrvavaddadyātpṛthagaṣṭaprakārataḥ  /
brāhmaṇānaṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayecca sadakṣiṇam  // 2,45.82 //
ekaṃ vā yoganirataṃ bhasmaniṣṭhaṃ jitendriyam  /
tryahaṃ caiva tu rudrasya mahācarunivedanam  // 2,45.83 //
viśeṣa evaṃ kathita aśeṣaśrāddhacoditaḥ  /
mṛte kuryānna kuryādvā jīvanmukto yataḥ svayam  // 2,45.84 //
nityanaimittikādīni kuryāddhā saṃttyajettu vā  /
bāndhave 'pi mṛte tasya śaucāśaucaṃ na vidyate  // 2,45.85 //
sūtakaṃ ca na saṃdehaḥ snānamātreṇa śuddhyati  /
paścājjāte kumāre ca sve kṣetre cātmano yadi  // 2,45.86 //
tasya sarvaṃ prakartavyaṃ putro 'pi brahmavidbhivet  /
kanyakā yadi rāñjātā paścāttasya mahātmanaḥ  // 2,45.87 //
ekaparṇā iva jñeyā aparṇā iva suvratā  /
bhavatyeva na saṃdehastasyāścānvayajā api  // 2,45.88 //
mucyante nātra saṃdehaḥ pitaro narakādapi  /
mucyante karmaṇānena mātṛtaḥ pitṛtastathā  // 2,45.89 //
kālaṃ gate dvije bhūmau khaneccāpi dahettu vā  /
putrakṛtyamaśeṣaṃ ca kṛtvā doṣo na vidyate  // 2,45.90 //
karmaṇā cottareṇaiva gatirasya na vidyate  /
brahmaṇākathitaṃ sarvaṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām  // 2,45.91 //
punaḥ sanatkumārāya kathitaṃ tena dhīmatā  /
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāyaiva kathitaṃ brahmasūnunā  // 2,45.92 //
prasādāttasya devasya vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ  /
jñātaṃ mayā kṛtaṃ caiva niyogādeva tasya tu  // 2,45.93 //
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ rahasyaṃ brahmasiddhidam  /
muniputrāya dātavyaṃ na cābhaktāya suvratāḥ  // 2,45.94 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge jīvacchrādvavidhirnāma pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
jīvacchrāddhavidhiḥ proktastvayā sūta mahāmate  /
mṛrkhāṇāmapi mokṣārthamasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa  // 2,46.1 //
rudrādityavasūnāṃ ca śakraādīnāṃ ca suvrata  /
pratiṣṭhā kīdṛśī śaṃbhorligamūrteśca śobhanā  // 2,46.2 //
viṣṇoḥ śakrasya devasya brahmaṇaśca mahātmanaḥ  /
agner yasya nirṛter varuṇasya mahādyuteḥ  // 2,46.3 //
vāyoḥ somasya yakṣasya kuberasyāmitātmanaḥ  /
īśānasya dharāyāśca śrīpratiṣṭhātha vā katham  // 2,46.4 //
durgāśivāpratiṣṭhā ca haimavatyāśca śobhanā  /
skandasya gaṇarājasya nandinaśca viśeṣataḥ  // 2,46.5 //
tathānyeṣāṃ ca devānāṃ gaṇānāmapi vā punaḥ  /
pratiṣṭhālakṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vistāradvaktumarhasi  // 2,46.6 //
bhavānsarvārthatattvajño rudrabhaktaśca suvrata  /
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasyāsi sākṣāttvamaparā tanuḥ  // 2,46.7 //
sumanturjaiminiścaiva pailaśca paramarṣayaḥ  /
gurubhaktiṃ tathā kartuṃ samartho romaharṣaṇaḥ  // 2,46.8 //
iti vyāsasya vipulā gāthā bhāgīrathītaṭe  /
ekaḥ samo vā bhinno vā śiṣyastasya mahādyuteḥ  // 2,46.9 //
vaiśaṃpāyanatulyo 'si vyāsaśiṣyeṣu bhūtale  /
tasmādasmākamakhilaṃ vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam  // 2,46.10 //
evamuktvā sthiteṣveva teṣu sarveṣu tatra ca  /
babhūva vismayo 'tīva munīnāṃ tasya cāgrataḥ  // 2,46.11 //
athāntarikṣe vipulā sākṣāddevī sarasvatī  /
alaṃ munīnāṃ praśro 'yamiti vācā babhūva ha  // 2,46.12 //
sarvaṃ liṅgamayaṃ lokaṃ sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam  /
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya sthāpayetpūjayecca tat  // 2,46.13 //
liṅgasthāpanasanmārganihitasvāyatāsinā  /
āśu brahmāṇḍamudbhidya nirgacchedaviśaṅkayā  // 2,46.14 //
upedrāṃbhojagarbhendrayamāṃbudhanadeśvarāḥ  /
tathānye ca śivaṃ sthāpya liṅgamūrti maheśvaram  // 2,46.15 //
sveṣusveṣu ca pakṣeṣu pradhānāste yathā dvijāḥ  /
brahmā haraśca bhagavānviṣṇurdevī ramā dharā  // 2,46.16 //
lakṣmīrdhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ prajñā dharā durgā śacī tathā  /
rudrāśca vasavaḥ skando viśākhaḥ śākha eva ca  // 2,46.17 //
naigameśaśca bhagavāṃllokapālā grahāstathā  /
sarve nandipurogāśca gaṇā gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ  // 2,46.18 //
pitaro munayaḥ sarve kuberādyāśca suprabhāḥ  /
āditya vasavaḥ sāṃkhyā aśvinau ca bhiṣagvarau  // 2,46.19 //
viśvedevāśca sādhyāśca paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo mṛgāḥ  /
brahmādisthāvarāntaṃ ca sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam  // 2,46.20 //
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya sthāpayelliṅgamavyayam  /
yatnena stāpitaṃ sarvaṃ pūjitaṃ pūjayedyadi  // 2,46.21 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
iti niśamya kṛtāñjalaya stadā divi mahāmunayaḥ kṛtaniścayāḥ  /
śivataraṃ śivamīśvaramavyayaṃ manasi liṅgamayaṃ praṇipatya te  // 2,47.1 //
sakaladevapatirbhagavānajo hariraśeṣapatirguruṇā svayam  /
munivarāśca gaṇāśca surāsurā naravarāḥ śivaliṅgamayāḥ punaḥ  // 2,47.2 //
śrutvaivaṃ munayaḥ sarve ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ  /
saṃtyajya sarvaṃ devasya pratiṣṭhāṃ kartumudyatāḥ  // 2,47.3 //
apṛcchansūtamanaghaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā  /
liṅgapratiṣṭhāṃ vipulāṃ sarve te śaṃsitavratāḥ  // 2,47.4 //
sūta uvāca
pratiṣṭhāṃ liṅgamūrtervo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  /
pravakṣyāmi samāsena dharmakāmārthamuktaye  // 2,47.5 //
kṛtvaiva liṅgaṃ vidhinā bhuvi liṅgeṣu yatnataḥ  /
liṅgamekatamaṃ śailaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam  // 2,47.6 //
hemaratnamayaṃ vāpi rājataṃ tāmrajaṃ tu vā  /
savedikaṃ sasūtraṃ ca samyagvistṛtamastakam  // 2,47.7 //
viśodhya sthāpayedbhaktyā savedikamanuttamam  /
liṅgavedī umā devī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ  // 2,47.8 //
tayoḥ sapūjanādeva devī devaśca pūjitau  /
pratiṣṭhayā ca deveśo devyā sārdhaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  // 2,47.9 //
tasmātsavedikaṃ liṅgaṃ sthāpayetsthāpakottamaḥ  // 2,47.10 //
mūle brahmā vasati bhagavānmadhyabhāge ca viṣṇuḥ sarveśānaḥ  /
paśupatirajo rudramūrtirvareṇyaḥ  /
tasmālliṅgaṃ gurutarataraṃ pūjayetsthāpayedvā yasmātpūjyo gaṇapatirasau devamukhyaiḥ samastaiḥ  // 2,47.11 //
gandhaiḥ sragdhūpadīpaiḥ snapanahutabalistotramantropahārairnityaṃ ye 'bhyarcayānti tridaśavaratanuṃ liṅgamūrtiṃ maheśam  /
garbhādhānādināśakṣayabhayarahitā devagandharvamukhyaiḥ siddhairvandyāśca pūjyā gaṇavaranamitāste bhavantyaprameyāḥ  // 2,47.12 //
tasmādbhaktyopacāreṇa sthāpayetparameśvaram  /
pūjayecca viśeṣeṇa liṅgaṃ sarvārthasiddhaye  // 2,47.13 //
samarcya sthāpayelliṅgaṃ tīrthamadhye śivāsane  /
kūrcavastrādibhirliṅgamācchādya kalaśaiḥ punaḥ  // 2,47.14 //
lokapālādidaivatyaiḥ sakūrcaiḥ sākṣataiḥ śubhaiḥ  /
utkūrcaiḥ svastikādyaiśca citratantukaveṣṭitaiḥ  // 2,47.15 //
vajrādikāyudopetaiḥ savastraiḥ sapidhānakaiḥ  /
lakṣayetparito liṅgamīśānena pratiṣṭhitam  // 2,47.16 //
dhūpadīpasamopetaṃ vitānavitatāṃbaram  /
lokapāladhvajaiścaiva gajādimahiṣādibhiḥ  // 2,47.17 //
citritaiḥ pūjitaiścaiva darbhamālā ca śobhanā  /
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā tayā bāhye ca veṣṭayet  // 2,47.18 //
tatodhivāsayettoye dhūpadīpasamanvite  /
pañcāhaṃ vā tryahaṃvātha ekarātramadhāpi vā  // 2,47.19 //
vedādhyayanasaṃpanno nṛtyagītādimaṅgalaiḥ  /
kiṅkiṇīravakopetaṃ tālavīṇāravairapi  // 2,47.20 //
īkṣayetkālamavyagro yajamānaḥ samāhitaḥ  /
utthāpya svastikaṃ dhyāyenmaṇḍape lakṣaṇānvite  // 2,47.21 //
saṃskṛte vedisaṃyukte navakuṇḍena saṃvṛte  /
pūrvokta vidhinā yukte sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyute  // 2,47.22 //
aṣṭamaṇḍalasaṃyukte digdhvajāṣṭakasaṃyute  /
pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaiḥ kuṇḍaiḥ prāgāditaḥ kramāt  // 2,47.23 //
pradhānaṃ kuṇḍamīśānyāṃ caturasraṃ vidhīyate  /
athavā pañcakuṇḍaikaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ caikameva ca  // 2,47.24 //
yajñopakaraṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ śivārcāyāṃ hi bhūṣaṇaiḥ  /
vedimadhye mahāśayyāṃ pañcatūlīprakalpitām  // 2,47.25 //
kalpayetkāñcanopetāṃ sitavastrāvaguṇṭhitām  /
prakalpyaivaṃ śivaṃ caiva sthāpayetparameśvaram  // 2,47.26 //
prākśiraskaṃ nyaselliṅgamīśānena yathāvidhi  /
ratnanyāse kṛte pūrva kevalaṃ kalaśaṃ nyaset  // 2,47.27 //
liṅgamācchādya vastrābhyāṃ kūrcena ca samantataḥ  /
ratnanyāse prasakte 'tha vāmādyā nava śaktayaḥ  // 2,47.28 //
navaratnaṃ hiraṇyādyaiḥ pañcagavyena saṃyutaiḥ  /
sarvadānyasamopetaṃ śilāyāmapi vinyaset  // 2,47.29 //
sthāpayedbrahmaliṅgaṃ hi śivagāyatrisaṃyutam  /
kevalaṃ praṇavenāpi sthāpayecchivamavyayam  // 2,47.30 //
brahmajajñānamantreṇa brahmabhāgaṃ prabhostathā  /
viṣṇugāyatriyā bhāgaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tvatha vinyaset  // 2,47.31 //
sūtre tattvatrayopete praṇavena pravinyaset  /
sarvaṃ namaḥ śivāyeti namo haṃsaḥ śivāya ca  // 2,47.32 //
rudrādhyāyena vā sarvaṃ parimṛjya ca vinyaset  /
sthāpayedbrahmabhiścaiva kalaśānvai samantataḥ  // 2,47.33 //
vedimadhye nyasetsarvānmūrvoktavidhisaṃyutān  /
madhyakuṃbhe śivaṃ devīṃ dakṣiṇe parameśvarīm  // 2,47.34 //
skandaṃ tayośca madhye tu skandakuṃbhe sucitrite  /
brahmāṇaṃ skandakuṃbhe vā īśakumbhe hariṃ tathā  // 2,47.35 //
athavā śivakuṃbhe ca brahmāṅgāni ca vinyaset  /
śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ  // 2,47.36 //
brahmāṇyevaṃ samāsena hṛdayādīni cāṃbikā  /
vedimadhye nyasetsarvānpūrvoktavidhisaṃyutān  // 2,47.37 //
vardhanyāṃ sthāpayeddevīṃ gandhatoyena pūrya ca  /
hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ ratnaṃ śivakuṃbhe pravinyaset  // 2,47.38 //
vardhanyāmāpi yatnena gāyatryaṅgaiśca suvratāḥ  /
vidyeśvarāndiśaṃ kuṃbhe brahmakūrcena pūrite  // 2,47.39 //
aṃnateśādidevāṃśca praṇavādinamontakam  /
navavastraṃ pratighaṭamaṣṭakuṃbheṣu dāpayet  // 2,47.40 //
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbheṣu hemaratnādi vinyaset  /
vaktrakrameṇa hotavyaṃ gāyatryaṅgakrameṇa ca  // 2,47.41 //
jayādisviṣṭaparyantaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret  /
secayecchivakuṃbhena vardhanyā vaiṣṇavena ca  // 2,47.42 //
paitā mahena kuṃbhena brahmabhāgaṃ viśeṣataḥ  /
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbhaiśca secayetparameśvaram  // 2,47.43 //
vinyasetsarvamantrāṇi pūrvavatsusamāhitaḥ  /
pūjayetsnapanaṃ kṛtvā sahasrādiṣu saṃbhavaiḥ  // 2,47.44 //
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā sahasrapaṇamuttamam  /
itareṣāṃ tadardhaṃ syāttadardhaṃ vā vidhīyate  // 2,47.45 //
vastrāṇi ca pradhānasya kṣetrabhūṣaṇagodhanam  /
utsavaśca prakartavyo homayagabaliḥ kramāt  // 2,47.46 //
navāhaṃ vāpi saptāhamekāhaṃ ca tryahaṃ tathā  /
homaśca pūrvavatprokto nityamabhyarcya śaṅkaram  // 2,47.47 //
devānāṃ bhāskarādīnāṃ homaṃ pūrvavadeva tu  /
abhyantare tathā bāhye vahnau nityaṃ samarcayet  // 2,47.48 //
ya evaṃ sthāpayelliṅgaṃ sa eva parameśvaraḥ  /
tena devagaṇā rudrā ṛṣayo 'psarasastathā  // 2,47.49 //
sthāpitāḥ pūjitāścaiva trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  // 2,47.50 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge liṅgasthāpanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ pratiṣṭhāmapi vistarāt  /
svairmatrairyāgakuṇḍāni vinyasyaikaikameva ca  // 2,48.1 //
sthāpayedutsavaṃ kṛtvā pūjayecca vidhānataḥ  /
bhānoḥ pañcāgninā kāryaṃ dvādaśāgnikrameṇa vā  // 2,48.2 //
sarvakuṇḍāni vṛttāni padmākārāṇi suvratāḥ  /
aṃbāyā yonikuṇḍaṃ syādvardhanyekā vidhīyate  // 2,48.3 //
śaktīnāṃ sarvakāryeṣu yonikuṇḍaṃ vidhīyate  /
gāyatrīṃ kalpayecchaṃbhoḥ sarveṣāmapi yatnataḥ  /
sarve rudrāṃśajā yasmātsaṃkṣepeṇa vadāmi vaḥ  // 2,48.4 //
gāyatrībhedāḥ
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi  /
tannaḥ śivaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.5 //
gaṇāṃbikāyai vidmahe karmasiddhyai ca dhīmahi  /
tanno gaurī pracodayāt  // 2,48.6 //
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe mahādevāya dhīmahi  /
tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.7 //
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vakratuṇḍāya dhīmahi  /
tanno dantiḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.8 //
mahāsenāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi  /
tannaḥ skandaḥ procadayāt  // 2,48.9 //
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe vedapādāya dhīmahi  /
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.10 //
harivaktrāya vidmahe rudravaktrāya dhīmahi  /
tanno nandī pracodayāt  // 2,48.11 //
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi  /
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.12 //
mahāṃbikāyai vidmahe karmasiddhaiya ca dhīmahi  /
tanno lakṣmīḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.13 //
samuddhṛtāyai vidmahe viṣṇunaikena dhīmahi  /
tanno dharā pracodayāt  // 2,48.14 //
vainateyāya vidmahe suvarṇapakṣāya dhīmahi  /
tanno garuḍaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.15 //
padmodbhavāya vidmahe vedavaktrāya dhīmahi  /
tannaḥ sraṣṭā pracodayāt  // 2,48.16 //
śivāsyajāyai vidmahe devarūpāyai dhīmahi  /
tanno vācā pracodayāt  // 2,48.17 //
devarājāya vidmahe vajrahastāya dhīmahi  /
tannaḥ śakraḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.18 //
rudranetrāya vidmahe śaktihastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno vahniḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.19 //
vaivasvatāya vidmahe daṇḍahastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno yamaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.20 //
niśācarāya vidmahe khaḍgahastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno nirṛtiḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.21 //
śuddhahastāya vidmahe pāśahastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno varuṇaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.22 //
sarpaprāṇāya vidmahe yaṣṭihastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno vuyaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.23 //
yakṣeśvarāya vidmahe gadāhastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno yakṣaḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.24 //
sarveśvarāya vidmahe śūlahastāya dhīmahi  /
tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt  // 2,48.25 //
kātyāyanyai vidmahe kanyākumāryai dhīmahi  /
tanno durgā pracodayāt  // 2,48.26 //
evaṃ prabhidya gāyatrīṃ tattadevānurūpataḥ  /
pūjayet sthāpayetteṣāmāsanaṃ praṇavaṃ smṛtam  // 2,48.27 //
athavā viṣṇumatulaṃ sūktena puruṣeṇa vā  /
viṣṇuṃ caiva mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāviṣṇumanukramāt  // 2,48.28 //
sthāpayeddevagāyatryā parikalpya vidhānataḥ  /
vāsudevaḥ pradhānastu tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ svayam  // 2,48.29 //
pradyumno hyaniruddhaśca mūrtibhedāstu vai prabhoḥ  /
bahūni vividhānīha tasya śāpodbhavāni ca  // 2,48.30 //
sarvāvarteṣu rūpāṇi jagatāṃ ca hitāya vai  /
matsyaḥ kūrmo 'tha vārāho nārasiṃho 'tha vāmanaḥ  // 2,48.31 //
rāmo rāmaśca kṛṣṇaśca bauddhaḥ kalkī tathaiva ca  /
tathānyāni na devasya hareḥ sāpodbhavāni ca  // 2,48.32 //
teṣāmapi ca gāyatrīṃ kṛtvā stāpya ca pūjayet  /
guhyāni devadevasya harernārāyaṇasya ca  // 2,48.33 //
vijñānāni ca yantrāṇi mantropaniṣadāni ca  /
pañca brahmāṅgajānīha pañcabhūtamayāni ca  // 2,48.34 //
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ paramaśobhanaḥ  /
hareraṣṭākṣarāṇīha praṇavena samāsataḥ  // 2,48.35 //
oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya ca  /
pradyumnāya pradhānāya aniruddhāya vai namaḥ  // 2,48.36 //
ekamekena mantreṇa sthāpayetparameśvaram  /
biṃbāniyāni devasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ  // 2,48.37 //
pratiṣṭhā caiva pūjā ca liṅgavanmunisattamāḥ  /
ratnavinyāsasahitaṃ kautukāni harerapi  // 2,48.38 //
acale kārayetsarvaṃ calepyevaṃ vidhānataḥ  /
tannetronmīlanaṃ kuryānnetramantreṇa suvratāḥ  // 2,48.39 //
kṣetrapradakṣiṇaṃ caiva ārāmasya purasya ca  /
jalādhivāsanaṃ caiva pūrvavatparikīrtitam  // 2,48.40 //
kuṇḍamaṇḍapanirmāṇaṃ śayanaṃ ca vidhīyate  /
hutvā navāgnibhāgena navakuṇḍe yatāvidhi  // 2,48.41 //
athavā pañcakuṇḍeṣu pradhāne kevale 'tha vā  /
pratiṣṭhā kathitā divyā pāraṃparyakramāgatā  // 2,48.42 //
śilodbhavānāṃ biṃbānāṃ citrābhāsasya vā punaḥ  /
jalādhivāsanaṃ proktaṃ vṛṣendrasya prakīrtitam  // 2,48.43 //
prāsādasya pratiṣṭhāyāṃ pratiṣṭhā parikīrtitā  /
prāsādāṅgasya sarvasya yathāṅgānāṃ tanoriva  // 2,48.44 //
vṛṣāgnimātṛvighneśakumārānapi yatnataḥ  /
śreṣṭhāṃ durgāṃ tathā caṇḍīṃ gāyatryā vai yathāvidhi  // 2,48.45 //
prāgādyaṃ sthāpayecchaṃbhoraṣṭāvaraṇamuttamam  /
lokapālagaṇeśādyānapi śaṃbhoḥ pravinyaset  // 2,48.46 //
umā caṇḍī ca nandī ca mahākālo mahāmuniḥ  /
vighneśvaro mahābhṛṅgī skandaḥ saumyāditaḥ kramāt  // 2,48.47 //
indrādīnsveṣu sthāneṣu brahmāṇaṃ ca janārdanam  /
sthāpayeccaiva yatnena kṣetreśaṃ veśagocare  // 2,48.48 //
siṃhāsane hyanantādīn vidyeśāmapi ca kramāt  /
sthāpayetpraṇavenaiva guhyāṅgādīni paṅkaje  // 2,48.49 //
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ calasthāpanasuttamam  /
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ devīnāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  // 2,48.50 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge 'ṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
aghoreśasya mahātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ purā  /
pūjāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ devasya bhagavanvaktumarhasi  // 2,49.1 //
sūta uvāca
aghoreṇāṅga yuktena vidhivacca viśeṣataḥ  /
pratiṣṭhāliṅgavidhinā nānyatā munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,49.2 //
tathāgnipūjāṃ vai kuryādyathā pūjā tathaiva ca  /
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā  // 2,49.3 //
tilairhemaḥ prakartavyo dadhimadhvājyasaṃyutaiḥ  /
ghṛtasaktumadūnāṃ ca sarvaduḥkhapramārjanam  // 2,49.4 //
vyādhīnāṃ nāśanaṃ caiva tilahomastu bhūtidaḥ  /
sahasreṇa mahābhūtiḥ śatena vyādhināśanam  // 2,49.5 //
sarvaduḥkhavinirmukto japena ca na saṃśayaḥ  /
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva trikāle ca yathāvidhi  // 2,49.6 //
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa ṣaṇmāsājjāyate dhruvam  /
siddhayo naiva saṃdeho rājyamaṇḍālināmapi  // 2,49.7 //
sahasreṇa jvaro yāti kṣīreṇa ca juhoti yam  /
trikālaṃ māsamekaṃ tu sahasraṃ juhuyātpayaḥ  // 2,49.8 //
māsena siddhyate tasya mahāsaubhāgyamuttamam  /
siddhyate cābdahomena kṣaudrājyadadhisaṃyutam  // 2,49.9 //
yavakṣīrājyahomena jātitaṇḍulakena vā  /
prīyeta bhagavānīśo hyaghoraḥ parameśvaraḥ  // 2,49.10 //
dadhnā puṣṭirnṛpāṇāṃ ca kṣīrahomena śāntikam  /
ṣaṇmāsaṃ tu ghṛtaṃ hutvā sarvavyādhivināśanam  // 2,49.11 //
rājayakṣmā tilairhemānnaśyate vatsareṇa tu  /
yavahomena cāyuṣyaṃ ghṛtena ca jayastadā  // 2,49.12 //
sarvakuṣṭhakṣayārthaṃ ca madhunāktaiśca taṇḍulaiḥ  /
juhuyādayutaṃ nityaṃ ṣaṇmāsānniyataḥ sadā  // 2,49.13 //
ājyaṅkṣīraṃ madhuścaiva madhuratrayamucyate  /
samastaṃ tuṣyate tasya nāśayedvai bhagandaram  // 2,49.14 //
kevalaṃ ghṛtahomena sarvarogakṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ  /
sarvavyādhi haraṃ dhyānaṃ sthāpanaṃ vidhinārcanam  // 2,49.15 //
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamaghorasya mahātmanaḥ  /
pratiṣṭhā yajanaṃ sarvaṃ nandinā kathitaṃ purā  // 2,49.16 //
brahmaputrāya śiṣyāya tena vyāsāya suvratāḥ  // 2,49.17 //

śrīlīṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nigrahaḥ kathitastena śivavaktreṇa śūlinā  /
kṛtāparāndhināṃ taṃ tu vaktumarhasi suvrata  // 2,50.1 //
tvayā navidinaṃ nāsti laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ tathā  /
śrautaṃ smārtaṃ mahābhāga romaharṣaṇa suvrata  // 2,50.2 //
sūta uvāca
purā bhṛgusutenokto hiraṇyākṣāya suvratāḥ  /
nigraho 'ghoraśiṣyeṇa śukreṇākṣayatejasā  // 2,50.3 //
tasya prasādaddaityendro hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān  /
trailokyamakhilaṃ jitvā sadevāsuramānuṣam  // 2,50.4 //
utpādya putraṃ gaṇapaṃ cāndhakaṃ cāruvikramam  /
rarāja loke devena varāheṇa niṣūditaḥ  // 2,50.5 //
strībādhāṃ bālabādhāṃ ca gavāmapi viśeṣataḥ  /
kurvato nāsti vijayo mārgeṇānena bhūtale  // 2,50.6 //
tena daityena sā devī dharā nītā rasātalam  /
tenāghoreṇa devena niṣphalo nigrahaḥ kṛtaḥ  // 2,50.7 //
saṃvatsara sahasrānte varāheṇa ca sūditaḥ  /
tasmādaghorasiddhyarthaṃ brāhmaṇānnaiva bādhayet  // 2,50.8 //
strīṇāmapi viśeṣeṇa gavāmapi na kārayet  /
guhyādguhyatamaṅgopyamatiguhyaṃ vadāmi vaḥ  // 2,50.9 //
ātatāyinamuddiśya kartavyaṃ nṛpasattamaiḥ  /
brāhmaṇebhyo na kartavyaṃ svarāṣṭreśasya vā punaḥ  // 2,50.10 //
atīvadurjaye prāpte bale sarve niṣūdite  /
adharmayuddhe saṃprāpte kuryādvidhimanuttamam  // 2,50.11 //
aghṛṇenaiva kartavyo hyaghṛṇenaiva kārayet  /
kṛtamātre na saṃdeho nigrahaḥ saṃprajāyate  // 2,50.12 //
lakṣamātraṃ pumāñjaptvā aghoraṃ ghorarūpiṇam  /
daśāṃśaṃ vidhinā hutvā tilena dvijasattamāḥ  // 2,50.13 //
saṃpūjya lakṣapuṣpeṇa sitena vidhipūrvakam  /
bāṇaliṅge 'thavā vahnau dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ  // 2,50.14 //
siddhamantro 'nyatā nāsti draṣṭā siddhyādayaḥ punaḥ  /
siddhamantraḥ svayaṃ kuryātpretasthāne viśeṣataḥ  // 2,50.15 //
mātṛsthāne 'pi vā vidvānvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ  /
kevalaṃ mantrasiddho vā brāhmaṇaḥ śivabhāvitaḥ  // 2,50.16 //
kuryādvidhimimaṃ dhīmānātmanor'thaṃ nṛpasya vā  /
sūlāṣṭakaṃ nyasedvidvānpūrvādīśānakāntakam  // 2,50.17 //
triśikhaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca caturviśācchikāgrataḥ  /
aghoravigrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃkalīkṛtavigrahaḥ  // 2,50.18 //
sarvanāśakaraṃ dhyātvā sarvakarmāṇi kārayet  /
kālāgnikoṭisaṃkāśaṃ svadehamapi bhāvayet  // 2,50.19 //
śūlaṃ kapālaṃ pāśaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ caiva śarāsanam  /
bāṇaṃ ḍamarukaṃ khaḍgamaṣṭāyudhamanukramāt  // 2,50.20 //
aṣṭahastaśca varado nīlakaṇṭho digaṃbaraḥ  /
pañcatattvasamārūḍho hyardhacandradharaḥ prabhuḥ  // 2,50.21 //
daṃṣṭrākarālavadano raudradṛṣṭirbhayaṅkaraḥ  /
huṃphaṭkāramahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukhaḥ  // 2,50.22 //
trinetraṃ nāgapāśena subaddhamukuṭaṃ svayam  /
sarvābharaṇasaṃpannaṃ pretabhasmāvaguṇṭhitam  // 2,50.23 //
bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiśca ḍākinībhiśca rākṣasaiḥ  /
saṃvṛtaṃ gajakṛttvā ca sarpabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam  // 2,50.24 //
vṛścikābharaṇaṃ devaṃ nīlanīradanisvanam  /
nīlāñjanādrisaṃkāśaṃ siṃhacarmottarīyakam  // 2,50.25 //
dhyāyedevamaghoreśaṃ ghoraghorataraṃ śivam  /
ṣaṭtriṃśaduktamātrābhiḥ prāṇāyāmena suvratāḥ  // 2,50.26 //
mahāmudrāsamāyuktaḥ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet  /
siddhamantraścitāgnau vā pretasthāne yathāvidhi  // 2,50.27 //
sthāpayenmadhyadeśe tu eendre yāmye ca vāruṇe  /
kauberyāṃ vidivatkṛtvā homakuṇḍāni śāstrataḥ  // 2,50.28 //
ācāryo madhyakuṇḍe tu sādhakāśca diśāsu vai  /
paristīrya vilomena pūrvavacchūlasaṃbhṛtaḥ  // 2,50.29 //
kālāgnipīṭhamadhyasthaḥ svayaṃ śiṣyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ  /
dhyātvā ghoramaghoreśaṃ dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃyutam  // 2,50.30 //
vibhītakena vai kṛtvā dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ  /
pīṭhe nyasya nṛpendrasya śatrumaṅgārakeṇa tu  // 2,50.31 //
kuṇḍasyādhaḥ khanecchatruṃ brāhmaṇaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ  /
adhomukhordhvapādaṃ tu sarvakuṇḍeṣu yatnataḥ  // 2,50.32 //
śmaśānāṅgāramānīya tuṣeṇa saha dāhayet  /
tatrāgniṃ sthāpayettūṣṇīṃ brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ  // 2,50.33 //
māyūrāstreṇa nābhyāṃ tu jvalanaṃ dīpayettataḥ  /
kañcukaṃ tuṣasaṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsāsthisamanvitaiḥ  // 2,50.34 //
raktavastrasamaṃ miśrairhemadravyairviśeṣataḥ  /
hastayantrodbhavaistailaiḥ saha homaṃ tu kārayet  // 2,50.35 //
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu homayedanupūrvaśaḥ  /
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ samārabhya yathākramam  // 2,50.36 //
aṣṭamyantaṃ tathāṅgāramaṇḍalasthānavarjitaḥ  /
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatravaḥ kulajaiḥ saha  // 2,50.37 //
sarvaduḥkhasamopetāḥ prayānti yamasādanam  /
mantreṇānena cādāya nṛkapāle nakhaṃ tathā  // 2,50.38 //
keśaṃ nṛṇāṃ tathāṅgāraṃ tuṣaṃ kañcukameva ca  /
cīracchaṭāṃ rājadhūlīṃ gṛhasaṃmārjanasya vā  // 2,50.39 //
viṣasarpasya dantāni vṛṣadantāni yāni tu  /
gavāṃ caiva krameṇaiva vyāghradantanakhāni ca  // 2,50.40 //
tathā kṛṣṇamṛgāṇāṃ ca biḍālasya ca pūrvavat  /
nakulasya ca dantāni varāhasya viśeṣataḥ  // 2,50.41 //
daṃṣṭrāṇi sādhayitvā tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ  /
japedaṣṭottaraśataṃ mantraṃ cāghoramuttamam  // 2,50.42 //
tatkapālaṃ nakhaṃ kṣetre gṛhe vā nagare 'pi vā  /
pretasthāne 'pi vā rāṣṭre mṛtavastreṇa veṣṭayet  // 2,50.43 //
śatroraṣṭamārāśau vā pariviṣṭe divākare  /
some vā pariviṣṭe tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ  // 2,50.44 //
sthānanāśo bhavettasya śatrornāśaśca jāyate  /
śatruṃ rājñaḥ samālikhya gamane samavasthite  // 2,50.45 //
bhūtale darpaṇaprakhye vitānopari śobhite  /
catustoraṇasaṃyukte darbhamālāsamāvṛte  // 2,50.46 //
vedādhyayanasaṃpanne rāṣṭre vṛddhiprakāśake  /
dakṣiṇena tu pādena mūrdhni saṃtāḍayetsvayam  // 2,50.47 //
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatrunāśo bhaviṣyati  /
svārāṣṭrapatimuddiśya yaḥ kuryādābhicārikam  // 2,50.48 //
sa ātmānaṃ nihatyaiva svakulaṃ nāśayetkudhīḥ  /
tasmātsvarāṣṭragāṃptāraṃ nṛpatiṃ pālayetsadā  // 2,50.49 //
mantraiṣadhikriyādyaiśca sarvayatnena sarvadā  /
etadrahasyaṃ kathitaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit  // 2,50.50 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nigraho 'ghorarūpeyaṃ kathito 'smākamuttamam  /
vajravāhanikāṃ vidyāṃ vaktumarhasi sattama  // 2,51.1 //
sūta uvāca
vajravāhanikā nāma sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī  /
anayā secayedvajraṃ nṛpāṇāṃ sādhayettathā  // 2,51.2 //
vajraṃ kṛtvā vidhānena tadvajramabhiṣicya ca  /
anayā vidyayā tasminvinyesetkāñcanena ca  // 2,51.3 //
tataścākṣaralakṣaṃ ca japedvidvānsamāhitaḥ  /
vajrīdaśāṃśaṃ juhuyādvajrakuṇḍe ghṛtādibhiḥ  // 2,51.4 //
tadvajraṃ gopayennityaṃ dāpayennṛpatestataḥ  /
tena vajreṇa vai gacchañchatrūñjīyādraṇājire  // 2,51.5 //
purā pitā mahenaiva labdhā vidyā prayatnataḥ  /
devī śakropakārārthaṃ sākṣādvajreśvarī tathā  // 2,51.6 //
purā tvaṣṭa prajānātho hataputraḥ sureśvarāt  /
vidyayāharataḥ somamindravaireṇa suvratāḥ  // 2,51.7 //
tasminyajñe yatāprāptaṃ vidinopakṛtaṃ haviḥ  /
tadaicchata mahābāhurviśvarūpavimardanaḥ  // 2,51.8 //
matputramavadhīḥ śakra na dāsye tava śobhanam  /
bhāgaṃ bhāgārhatā naiva viśvarūpo hatastvayā  // 2,51.9 //
ityuktvā cāśramaṃ sarvaṃ mohayāmāsa māyayā  /
tato māyāṃ vinirbhidya viśvarūpavimardanaḥ  // 2,51.10 //
prasahya somamapibatsagaṇaiśca śacīpatiḥ  /
tatastaccheṣamādāya krodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ  // 2,51.11 //
indrasya śatro vardhasva svāhetyagnau juhāva ha  /
tataḥ kālāgnisaṃkāśo vartanādvṛtrasaṃjñitaḥ  // 2,51.12 //
prādurāsīt sureśārir dudrāva ca vṛṣāntakaḥ  /
tataḥ kirīṭī bhagavānparityajya divaṃ kṣaṇāt  // 2,51.13 //
sahasranetraḥ sagaṇo dudrāva bhayavihvalaḥ  /
tadā tamāha sa vibhṛrhṛṣṭo brahmā ca viśvasṛṭ  // 2,51.14 //
tyaktvā vajraṃ tametena jahītyarisarindamaḥ  /
so 'pi sannahya devendro devaiḥ sārdhaṃ mahābhujaḥ  // 2,51.15 //
nihatya cāprayatnena gatavānvigatajvaraḥ  /
tasmādvajreśvarīvidyā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī  // 2,51.16 //
mandehā rākṣasā nityaṃ vijitā vidyayaiva tu  /
tāṃ vidyāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapramocanīm  // 2,51.17 //
oṃ bhūrbhuvasvaḥ tatsaviturvareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi  /
dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt  /
oṃ phaṭ jahi huṃ phaṭ chindhi bhindhi jahi hanahana svāhā  /
vidyā vajreśvarītyeṣā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī  /
anayā saṃhṛtiḥ śaṃbhorvidyāyā munipuṅgavāḥ  // 2,51.18 //

iti śrīliṃṅgamahāpārāṇe uttarabhāge ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrutā vajreśvarī vidyā brāhmī śakropakāriṇī  /
anayā sarvakāryāṇi nṛpāmāmiti naḥ śrutam  // 2,52.1 //
viniyogaṃ vadasvāsyā vidyāyā romaharṣaṇa  /
sūta uvāca
vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ caiva vidveṣaṇamataḥ param  // 2,52.2 //
uccāṭanaṃ staṃbhanaṃ ca mohanaṃ tāḍanaṃ tathā  /
utsādanaṃ tathā chedaṃ māraṇaṃ pratibandhanam  // 2,52.3 //
senāstaṃbhanakādīni sāvitryā sarvamācaret  /
āgaccha varade devi bhūmyāṃ parvatamūrdhani  // 2,52.4 //
brāhmaṇebyo hyanujñātā gaccha devi yathāsukham  /
udvāsyānena mantreṇa gantavyaṃ nānyathā dvijāḥ  // 2,52.5 //
pratikāryaṃ tathā bāhyaṃ kṛtvā paśyādikāṃ kriyām  /
udvāsya vahnimādhāya punaranyaṃ yathāvidhi  // 2,52.6 //
devīmāvāhya ca punarjapetsaṃpūjayetpunaḥ  /
homaṃ ca vidhinā vahnau punareva samācaret  // 2,52.7 //
sarvakāryāṇi vidhinā sādhayedvidyayā punaḥ  /
jātīpuṣpaiśca vaśyārthi juhuyādayutatrayam  // 2,52.8 //
ghṛtena karavīreṇa kuryādākarṣaṇaṃ dvijāḥ  /
vidveṣaṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa kuryāllāṅgalakasya ca  // 2,52.9 //
tailenoccāṭanaṃ proktaṃ staṃbhanaṃ madhunā smṛtam  /
tilena mohanaṃ proktaṃ tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa ca  // 2,52.10 //
kharasya ca gajasyātha uṣṭrasya ca yathākramam  /
staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi pāṭanaṃ cākuśena ca  // 2,52.11 //
māraṇoccāṭane caiva rohībījena suvratāḥ  /
bandhanantvahipatreṇa senāstaṃbhamataḥ param  // 2,52.12 //
kunaṭyā niyataṃ vidyātpūjayetparameśvarīm  /
ghṛtena sarvasiddhiḥ syātpayasā vā viśuddhyate  // 2,52.13 //
tilena roganāśaśca kamalena dhanaṃ bhavet  /
kāntirmadhūkapuṣpeṇa sāvitryā hyayutatrayam  // 2,52.14 //
jayādiprabhṛtīnsarvān sviṣṭāntaṃ pūrvavatsmṛtam  /
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto viniyogotivistṛtaḥ  // 2,52.15 //
japedvā kevalāṃ vidyāṃ saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ  /
sarvasiddhimavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  // 2,52.16 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ

________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ sūta brahmakṣatraviśāmapi  /
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ sarvajño 'si mahāmate  // 2,53.1 //
suta uvāca
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ vakṣye bahunā kiṃ dvijottamāḥ  /
rudrādhyāyena vidhinā ghṛtena niyutaṃ kramāt  // 2,53.2 //
saghṛtena tilenaiva kamalena prayatnataḥ  /
dūrvayā ghṛtagokṣīramiśrayā madhunā tathā  // 2,53.3 //
caruṇā saghṛtenaiva kevalaṃ payasāpi vā  /
juhuyātkāla mṛtyorvā pratīkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ  // 2,53.4 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


sūta uvāca
triyaṃbakeṇa mantreṇa devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam  /
pūjayedbāṇaliṅge vā svayaṃbhūte 'pi vā punaḥ  // 2,54.1 //
āyurvedavidairvāpi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  /
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa puṇḍarīkeṇa śaṅkaram  // 2,54.2 //
kamalena sahasreṇa tathā nīlotpalena vā  /
saṃpūjya pāyasaṃ dattvā saghṛtaṃ caudanaṃ punaḥ  // 2,54.3 //
mudgānnaṃ madhunā yuktaṃ bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca  /
agnau homaśca vipulo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  // 2,54.4 //
pūrvoktairapi puṣpaiśca caruṇā ca viśeṣataḥ  /
japedvai niyutaṃ samyak samāpya ca yathākramam  // 2,54.5 //
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayedvai sadakṣiṇam  /
gavāṃ sahasraṃ dattvā tu hiraṇyamapi dāpayet  // 2,54.6 //
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sarahasyaṃ samāsataḥ  /
śivena devadevena śarveṇātyugraśūlinā  // 2,54.7 //
kathitaṃ meruśikhare skandāyāmitatejase  /
skandena devadevena brahmaputrāya dhīmate  // 2,54.8 //
sākṣātsanatkumāreṇa sarvalokahitaiṣiṇā  /
pārāśaryāya kathitaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam  // 2,54.9 //
śuke gate parandhāma dṛṣṭvā rudraṃ triyaṃbakam  /
gataśoko mahābhāgo vyasaḥ para ṛṣiḥ prabhuḥ  // 2,54.10 //
skandasya saṃbhavaṃ śrutvā sthitāya ca mahātmane  /
triyaṃbakasya māhātmyaṃ mantrasya ca viśeṣataḥ  // 2,54.11 //
kathitaṃ bahudhā tasmai kṛṣṇadvaipāyānāya vai  /
tatsakvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi prasādādeva tasya vai  // 2,54.12 //
devaṃ saṃpūjya vidhinā japenmantraṃ triyaṃbakam  /
mucyate sarpapāpaiśca saptajanmakṛtairapi  // 2,54.13 //
saṃgrāme tatsarvaṃ labdhvā saubhāgyamatulaṃ bhavet  /
lakṣahomena rājyārthī rājyaṃ labdhvā sukhī bhavet  // 2,54.14 //
putrārthī putramāpnoti niyutena na saṃśayaḥ  /
dhanārthī prayutenaiva japedeva na saṃśayaḥ  // 2,54.15 //
dhanadhānyādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ saṃpūrṇaḥ sarvamaṅgalaiḥ  /
krīḍate putrapautraiśca mṛtaḥ svarge prajāyate  // 2,54.16 //
nānena sadṛśo mantro loke vede ca suvratāḥ  /
tasmāttriyaṃbakaṃ devaṃ tena nityaṃ prapūjayet  // 2,54.17 //
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet  /
trayāṇāmapi lokānāṃ guṇānāmapi yaḥ prabhuḥ  // 2,54.18 //
vedānāmapi devānāṃ brahmakṣatraviśāmapi  /
akārokāramakārāṇāṃ mātrāṇāmapi vācakaḥ  // 2,54.19 //
tathā somasya sūryasya vahneragnitrayasya ca  /
aṃbā umā mahādevo hyaṃbakastu triyaṃbakaḥ  // 2,54.20 //
supuṣpitasya vṛkṣasya yathā gandhaḥ suśobhanaḥ  /
vāti dvarāttathā tasya gandhaḥ śaṃbhormahātmanaḥ  // 2,54.21 //
tasmātsugandho bhagavāngandhārayati śaṅkaraḥ  /
gāndhāraścamahādevo devānāmapi līlayā  // 2,54.22 //
sugandhastasya lokesminvāyurvāti nabhastale  /
tasmātsugandhistaṃ devaṃ sugandhi puṣṭivardhanam  // 2,54.23 //
yasya retaḥ purā śaṃbhorhareryonau pratiṣṭhitam  /
tasya vīryādabhūdaṇḍaṃ hiraṇmayam ajodbhavam  // 2,54.24 //
candrādityau sanakṣatrau bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahastapaḥ  /
satyalokamatikramya puṣṭirvīryasya tasya vai  // 2,54.25 //
pañcabhūtānyahaṅkāro buddhiḥ prakṛtireva ca  /
puṣṭirbījasya tasyaiva tasmādvai puṣṭivardhanaḥ  // 2,54.26 //
taṃ puṣṭivardhanaṃ devaṃ ghṛtena payasā tathā  /
madhunā yavagodhūmamāṣabilvaphalena ca  // 2,54.27 //
kumudārkaśamīpatragaurasarṣapaśālibhiḥ  /
hutvā liṅge yathānyāyaṃ bhaktyā devaṃ yajāmahe  // 2,54.28 //
ṛtenānena māṃ pāśādbandhanātkarmayogataḥ  /
mṛtyośca bandanāccaiva mukṣīya bhava tejasā  // 2,54.29 //
urvārukāṇāṃ pakvānāṃ yathā kālādabhūtpunaḥ  /
tathaiva kālaḥ saṃprāpto manunā tena yatnataḥ  // 2,54.30 //
evaṃ mantravidhiṃ jñātvā śivaliṅgaṃ samarcayet  /
tasya pāśakṣayo 'tīva yogino mṛtyunigrahaḥ  // 2,54.31 //
triyaṃbakasamo nāsti devo vā ghṛṇayānvitaḥ  /
prasādaśīlaḥ prītaśca tathā mantropi suvratāḥ  // 2,54.32 //
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya triyaṃbakamumāpatim  /
triyaṃbakeṇa mantreṇa pūjayetsusamāhitaḥ  // 2,54.33 //
sarvāvasthāṃ gato vāpi mukto 'yaṃ sarvapātakaiḥ  /
śivadhyānānna saṃdeho yathā rudrastathā svayam  // 2,54.34 //
hatvā bhittvā ca bhūtāni bhuktvā cānyāyato 'pi vā  /
śivamekaṃ sakṛtsmṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  // 2,54.35 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge cutaṣpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


________________________________________________________


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ triyaṃbako devo devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ  /
dhyeyaḥ sarvārthāsiddhyarthaṃ yogamārgeṇa suvrata  // 2,55.1 //
pūrvamevāpi nikhilaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ punaḥ  /
vistareṇa ca tatsarvaṃ saṃkṣepādvaktumarhasi  // 2,55.2 //
sūta uvāca
evaṃ paitāmahenaiva nandī dinakaraprabhaḥ  /
merupṛṣṭhe purā pṛṣṭo munisaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ  // 2,55.3 //
so 'pi tasmai kumārāya brahmaputrāya suvratāḥ  /
mithaḥ provāca bhagavānpraṇatāya samāhitaḥ  // 2,55.4 //
nandikeśvara uvāca
evaṃ purā mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ  /
giriputryāṃbayā devyā bhagavatyaikaśayyayā  // 2,55.5 //
pṛṣṭaḥ kailāsaśikhare hṛṣṭapuṣṭatanūruhaḥ  /
śrīdevyuvāca
yogaḥ katividhaḥ proktastatkathaṃ caiva kīdṛśam  // 2,55.6 //
jñānaṃ ca mokṣadaṃ divyaṃ mucyante yena jantavaḥ  /
śrībhagavānuvāca
prathamo mantrayogaśca sparśayogo dvitīyakaḥ  // 2,55.7 //
bhāvayogastṛtīyaḥ syād abhāvaśca caturthakaḥ  /
sarvottamo mahāyogaḥ pañcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  // 2,55.8 //
dhyānayukto japābhyāso mantrayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  /
nāḍīśuddhyadhiko yastu recakādikramānvitaḥ  // 2,55.9 //
samastavyastayogena jayo vāyoḥ prakīrtitaḥ  /
balasthirakriyāyukto dhāraṇādyaiśca śobhanaiḥ  // 2,55.10 //
dhāraṇātrayasaṃdīpto bhedatrayaviśodhakaḥ  /
kuṃbhakāvasthito 'bhyāsaḥ sparśayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  // 2,55.11 //
mantrasparśavinirmukto mahādevaṃ samāśritaḥ  /
bahirantarvibhāgasthasphuratsaṃharaṇātmakaḥ  // 2,55.12 //
bhāvayogaḥ samākhyātāścittaśuddhipradāyakaḥ  /
vilināvayavaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam  // 2,55.13 //
śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ nirābhāsaṃ svarūpaṃ yatra cintyate  /
abhāvayogaḥ saṃproktaścittanirvāṇakārakaḥ  // 2,55.14 //
nīrūpaḥ kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ svacchandaṃ ca suśobhanaḥ  /
anirdeśyaḥ sadālokaḥ svayaṃvedyaḥ samaṃ tataḥ  // 2,55.15 //
svabhāvo bhāsate yatra mahāyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  /
nityoditaḥ svayañjyotiḥ sarvacittasamutthitaḥ  // 2,55.16 //
nirmalaḥ kevalo hyātmā mahāyoga iti smṛtaḥ  /
aṇimādipradāḥ sarve sarve jñānasya dāyakāḥ  // 2,55.17 //
uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyameṣu yogeṣvanukramāt  /
ahaṃ saṃgavinirmukto mahākāśopamaḥ paraḥ  // 2,55.18 //
sarvāvaraṇanirmukto hyacintyaḥ svarasena tu  /
jñeyametatsamākhyātamagrāhyamapi daivataiḥ  // 2,55.19 //
pravilīno mahānsamyak svayaṃvedyaḥ svasākṣikaḥ  /
cakāstyānandavapuṣā tena jñeyam idaṃ matam  // 2,55.20 //
parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye  /
dhārmikāyākṛtaghnāya dātavyaṃ kramapūrvakam  // 2,55.21 //
gurudaivatabhaktāya anyathā naiva dāpayet  /
nindito vyādhitolpāyustathā caiva prajāyate  // 2,55.22 //
dāturapyevamanaghe tasmājñātvaiva dāpayet  /
sarvasaṃgavinirmukto madbhakto matparāyaṇaḥ  // 2,55.23 //
sādhako jñānasaṃyuktaḥ śrautasmārtaviśāradaḥ  /
gurubhaktaśca puṇyātmā yogyo yogarataḥ sadā  // 2,55.24 //
eva devi samākhyāto yogamārgaḥ sanātanaḥ  /
sarvavedāgamāṃbhojamakarandaḥ sumadhyame  // 2,55.25 //
pītvā yogāmṛtaṃ yogī mucyate brahmavittamaḥ  /
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ yogaiśvaryamanuttamam  // 2,55.26 //
atyāśramamidaṃ jñeyaṃ muktaye kena labhyate  /
tasmādiṣṭaiḥ samācāraiḥ śivārcanarataiḥ priye  // 2,55.27 //
ityuktvā bhagavāndevīmanujñāpya vṛṣadhvajaḥ  /
śaṅkukarṇaṃ samāsādya yuyojātmānamātmani  // 2,55.28 //
śailādiruvāca
tasmāttvamapi yogīndra yogābhyāsarato bhava  /
svaṃyabhuva parā mūrtirnūnaṃ brahmamayī varā  // 2,55.29 //
tasmātsarvaprayatnena mokṣārtho puruṣottamaḥ  /
bhasmasnāyī bhavennityaṃ yoge pāśupate rataḥ  // 2,55.30 //
dhyeyā yathākrameṇaiva vaiṣṇavī ca tataḥ parā  /
māheśvarī parā paścātsaiva dhyeyā yathākramam  // 2,55.31 //
yogeśvarasya yā niṣṭhā saiṣā saṃhṛtya varṇitā  // 2,55.32 //
sūta uvāca
evaṃ śilādaputreṇa nandinā kulanandinā  /
yogaḥ pāśupataḥ prokto bhasmaniṣṭhena dhīmatā  // 2,55.33 //
sanatkumāro bhagavānvyāsāyāmitatejase  /
tasmādahamapi śrutvā niyogātsatriṇāmapi  // 2,55.34 //
kṛtakṛtyo 'smi viprebhyo namo yajñebhya eva ca  /
namaḥ śivāya śāntāya vyāsāya munaye namaḥ  // 2,55.35 //
granthaikādaśasāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgamuttamam  /
aṣṭottarasatādhyāya mādimāṃśamataḥ param  // 2,55.36 //
ṣaṭcatvārīṃśadadhyāyaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam  /
atha te munayaḥ sarve naimiṣeyāḥ samāhitāḥ  // 2,55.37 //
praṇemurdevamīśānaṃ prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ  /
śākhāṃ paurāṇikīmevaṃ kṛtvaikādaśikāṃ prabhuḥ  // 2,55.38 //
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavānidaṃ vacanamabravīt  /
laiṅgamādyantamakhilaṃ yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi  // 2,55.39 //
dvijebhyaḥ śrāvayedvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  /
tapasā caiva yajñena dānenādhyayanena ca  // 2,55.40 //
yā gatistasya vipulā śāstravidyā ca vaidikī  /
karmaṇā cāpi miśreṇa kevalaṃ vidyayāpi vā  // 2,55.41 //
nivṛttiścāsya viprasya bhavedbhaktiśca śāśvatī  /
mayi nārāyaṇe deve śraddhā cāstu mahātmanaḥ  // 2,55.42 //
vaṃśasya cākṣayā vidyā cāpramādaśca sarvataḥ  /
ityājñā brahmaṇastasmāttasya sarvaṃ mahātmanaḥ  // 2,55.43 //
ṛṣayaḥ procuḥ
ṛṣeḥ sūtasya cāsmākameteṣābhapi cāsya ca  /
nāradasya ca yā siddhistīrthayātrāratasya ca  // 2,55.44 //
prītiśca vipulā yasmā dasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa  // 2,55.45 //
sā sadāstu virūpākṣaprasādāttu samantataḥ  /
evamukteṣu vipreṣu nārado bhagavānapi  // 2,55.46 //
karābhyāṃ suśubhāgrābhyāṃ sūtaṃ pasparśivāṃstvaci  /
svastyastu sūta bhadraṃ te mahādeve vṛṣadhvaje  // 2,55.47 //
śraddhā tavāstu cāsmākaṃ namastasmai śivāya ca  // 2,55.48 //

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcapañcāśattamodhyāyaḥ

samāptaṃ caitallaiṅgottarārdham

śrībhavānīśaṅkarārpaṇamastu
